**Cursor**

ë¬¸ì œë¥¼ ì°¾ì•˜ìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤! ë‘ ê°€ì§€ ì˜¤ë¥˜ê°€ ìˆìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤:

## ğŸ” **ë¬¸ì œ 1: ìŠ¤í”„ë ˆë“œì‹œíŠ¸ í—¤ë” ì˜¤íƒ€**
- **ìŠ¤í”„ë ˆë“œì‹œíŠ¸**: `'appicationUrl'` (iê°€ ë¹ ì§)
- **ìŠ¤í¬ë¦½íŠ¸ ê¸°ëŒ€ê°’**: `'applicationUrl'`

## ğŸ” **ë¬¸ì œ 2: ë§¤í•‘ ë¡œì§ ì˜¤ë¥˜**
ìŠ¤í¬ë¦½íŠ¸ê°€ `appicationUrl`ì„ `applicationUrl`ë¡œ ë§¤í•‘í•˜ì§€ ëª»í•˜ê³  ìˆìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤.

## ğŸ”§ **í•´ê²° ë°©ë²•**

```javascript
const fs = require('fs');
const axios = require('axios');

// Google Sheets APIë¥¼ í†µí•´ ë°ì´í„° ê°€ì ¸ì˜¤ê¸°
async function fetchSheetData(sheetId, range, apiKey) {
  const url = `https://sheets.googleapis.com/v4/spreadsheets/${sheetId}/values/${range}?key=${apiKey}`;
  
  try {
    const response = await axios.get(url);
    return response.data.values;
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('ì‹œíŠ¸ ë°ì´í„° ê°€ì ¸ì˜¤ê¸° ì‹¤íŒ¨:', error.message);
    throw error;
  }
}

// ë°°ì—´ ë°ì´í„°ë¥¼ JSON ê°ì²´ë¡œ ë³€í™˜
function convertRowsToObjects(rows) {
  if (!rows || rows.length < 2) return [];
  
  const headers = rows[0];
  const dataRows = rows.slice(1);
  
  return dataRows.map(row => {
    const obj = {};
    headers.forEach((header, index) => {
      let value = row[index] || '';
      
      // í—¤ë”ëª… ì •ê·œí™” (ëŒ€ë¬¸ì -> ì†Œë¬¸ì, íŠ¹ìˆ˜ ì¼€ì´ìŠ¤ ì²˜ë¦¬)
      let normalizedHeader = header.toLowerCase();
      
      // applicationUrl ë§¤í•‘ (ì˜¤íƒ€ ì¼€ì´ìŠ¤ í¬í•¨)
      if (normalizedHeader === 'applicationurl' || normalizedHeader === 'appicationurl') {
        normalizedHeader = 'applicationUrl';
      }
      if (normalizedHeader === 'createdat') {
        normalizedHeader = 'createdAt';
      }
      if (normalizedHeader === 'updatedat') {
        normalizedHeader = 'updatedAt';
      }
      if (normalizedHeader === 'detaileddescription') {
        normalizedHeader = 'detailedDescription';
      }
      
      // íŠ¹ë³„ ì²˜ë¦¬ê°€ í•„ìš”í•œ í•„ë“œë“¤
      if (normalizedHeader === 'situations' || normalizedHeader === 'tags') {
        // ì½¤ë§ˆë¡œ êµ¬ë¶„ëœ ë¬¸ìì—´ì„ ë°°ì—´ë¡œ ë³€í™˜
        value = value.split(',').map(item => item.trim()).filter(item => item);
      } else if (normalizedHeader === 'views') {
        // ìˆ«ì ë³€í™˜
        value = parseInt(value) || 0;
      } else if (normalizedHeader === 'deadline') {
        // ë‚ ì§œ í˜•ì‹ ê²€ì¦ (YYYY-MM-DD)
        if (value && !value.match(/^\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2}$/)) {
          console.warn(`ì˜ëª»ëœ ë‚ ì§œ í˜•ì‹: ${value}`);
        }
      }
      
      // ì •ê·œí™”ëœ í—¤ë”ëª…ìœ¼ë¡œ ì €ì¥
      obj[normalizedHeader] = value;
    });
    return obj;
  });
}

// ë°ì´í„° ê²€ì¦
function validatePolicyData(policies) {
  // í˜„ì¬ ìŠ¤í”„ë ˆë“œì‹œíŠ¸ì— ìˆëŠ” í•„ìˆ˜ í•„ë“œë“¤ë§Œ ì²´í¬
  const requiredFields = ['id', 'title', 'summary', 'category', 'source', 'tags', 'situations', 'target', 'amount', 'deadline', 'applicationUrl'];
  const errors = [];
  
  policies.forEach((policy, index) => {
    requiredFields.forEach(field => {
      if (!policy[field]) {
        errors.push(`ì •ì±… ${index + 1}: ${field} í•„ë“œê°€ ë¹„ì–´ìˆìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤.`);
      }
    });
    
    // URL í˜•ì‹ ê²€ì¦
    if (policy.applicationUrl && !policy.applicationUrl.startsWith('http')) {
      errors.push(`ì •ì±… ${index + 1}: applicationUrlì´ ì˜¬ë°”ë¥¸ URL í˜•ì‹ì´ ì•„ë‹™ë‹ˆë‹¤.`);
    }
    
    // ì¹´í…Œê³ ë¦¬ ê²€ì¦
    const validCategories = ['housing', 'employment-education', 'welfare', 'finance-startup', 'medical'];
    if (policy.category && !validCategories.includes(policy.category)) {
      errors.push(`ì •ì±… ${index + 1}: ìœ íš¨í•˜ì§€ ì•Šì€ ì¹´í…Œê³ ë¦¬ì…ë‹ˆë‹¤. (${policy.category})`);
    }
  });
  
  return errors;
}

async function main() {
  const apiKey = process.env.SHEETS_API_KEY;
  const sheetId = process.env.SHEETS_ID;
  
  if (!apiKey || !sheetId) {
    throw new Error('GOOGLE_SHEETS_API_KEY ë˜ëŠ” GOOGLE_SHEETS_ID í™˜ê²½ë³€ìˆ˜ê°€ ì„¤ì •ë˜ì§€ ì•Šì•˜ìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤.');
  }
  
  try {
    console.log('ğŸ“Š Google Sheetsì—ì„œ ì •ì±… ë°ì´í„°ë¥¼ ê°€ì ¸ì˜¤ëŠ” ì¤‘...');
    
    // ì •ì±… ë°ì´í„° ê°€ì ¸ì˜¤ê¸°
    const policyRows = await fetchSheetData(sheetId, 'ì •ì±…_ë§ˆìŠ¤í„°!A:Z', apiKey);
    
    // ë””ë²„ê¹…: í—¤ë”ì™€ ì²« ëª‡ í–‰ ì¶œë ¥
    console.log('ğŸ“‹ ìŠ¤í”„ë ˆë“œì‹œíŠ¸ í—¤ë”:', policyRows[0]);
    console.log('ğŸ“‹ ë°ì´í„° í–‰ ìˆ˜:', policyRows.length);
    if (policyRows.length > 1) {
      console.log('ğŸ“‹ ì²« ë²ˆì§¸ ë°ì´í„° í–‰:', policyRows[1]);
    }
    
    const policies = convertRowsToObjects(policyRows);
    
    // ìƒí™© ë°ì´í„° ê°€ì ¸ì˜¤ê¸° (ì„ íƒì‚¬í•­)
    let situations = [];
    try {
      const situationRows = await fetchSheetData(sheetId, 'ìƒí™©ë°ì´í„°!A:Z', apiKey);
      situations = convertRowsToObjects(situationRows);
    } catch (error) {
      console.warn('ìƒí™© ë°ì´í„° ì‹œíŠ¸ë¥¼ ì°¾ì„ ìˆ˜ ì—†ìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤. ê¸°ì¡´ ë°ì´í„°ë¥¼ ìœ ì§€í•©ë‹ˆë‹¤.');
      // ê¸°ì¡´ situations.json íŒŒì¼ ìœ ì§€
      if (fs.existsSync('src/data/situations.json')) {
        const existingData = JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync('src/data/situations.json', 'utf8'));
        situations = existingData.situations || [];
      }
    }
    
    // ë°ì´í„° ê²€ì¦
    const errors = validatePolicyData(policies);
    if (errors.length > 0) {
      console.error('âŒ ë°ì´í„° ê²€ì¦ ì‹¤íŒ¨:');
      errors.forEach(error => console.error(`  - ${error}`));
      process.exit(1);
    }
    
    // JSON íŒŒì¼ ìƒì„±
    const policiesData = { policies };
    const situationsData = { situations };
    
    fs.writeFileSync('src/data/policies.json', JSON.stringify(policiesData, null, 2));
    if (situations.length > 0) {
      fs.writeFileSync('src/data/situations.json', JSON.stringify(situationsData, null, 2));
    }
    
    console.log(`âœ… ì„±ê³µì ìœ¼ë¡œ ì—…ë°ì´íŠ¸ë˜ì—ˆìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤:`);
    console.log(`  - ì •ì±… ë°ì´í„°: ${policies.length}ê°œ`);
    console.log(`  - ìƒí™© ë°ì´í„°: ${situations.length}ê°œ`);
    
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('âŒ ì—…ë°ì´íŠ¸ ì‹¤íŒ¨:', error.message);
    process.exit(1);
  }
}

main();

```

ì¶”ê°€ë¡œ ë””ë²„ê¹… ë¡œê·¸ë¥¼ ê°œì„ í•´ì„œ ë§¤í•‘ì´ ì œëŒ€ë¡œ ë˜ëŠ”ì§€ í™•ì¸í•˜ê² ìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤:

```javascript
}

// ë°ì´í„° ê²€ì¦
function validatePolicyData(policies) {
  // í˜„ì¬ ìŠ¤í”„ë ˆë“œì‹œíŠ¸ì— ìˆëŠ” í•„ìˆ˜ í•„ë“œë“¤ë§Œ ì²´í¬

    requiredFields.forEach(field => {
      if (!policy[field]) {
        errors.push(`ì •ì±… ${index + 1}: ${field} í•„ë“œê°€ ë¹„ì–´ìˆìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤.`);

async function main() {
  const apiKey = process.env.SHEETS_API_KEY;
  const sheetId = process.env.SHEETS_ID;
  
  if (!apiKey || !sheetId) {
    throw new Error('GOOGLE_SHEETS_API_KEY ë˜ëŠ” GOOGLE_SHEETS_ID í™˜ê²½ë³€ìˆ˜ê°€ ì„¤ì •ë˜ì§€ ì•Šì•˜ìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤.');
  }
  
  try {
    console.log('ğŸ“Š Google Sheetsì—ì„œ ì •ì±… ë°ì´í„°ë¥¼ ê°€ì ¸ì˜¤ëŠ” ì¤‘...');
    
    // ì •ì±… ë°ì´í„° ê°€ì ¸ì˜¤ê¸°
    const policyRows = await fetchSheetData(sheetId, 'ì •ì±…_ë§ˆìŠ¤í„°!A:Z', apiKey);
    
    // ë””ë²„ê¹…: í—¤ë”ì™€ ì²« ëª‡ í–‰ ì¶œë ¥
    console.log('ğŸ“‹ ìŠ¤í”„ë ˆë“œì‹œíŠ¸ í—¤ë”:', policyRows[0]);
    console.log('ğŸ“‹ ë°ì´í„° í–‰ ìˆ˜:', policyRows.length);
    if (policyRows.length > 1) {
      console.log('ğŸ“‹ ì²« ë²ˆì§¸ ë°ì´í„° í–‰:', policyRows[1]);
    }
    
    const policies = convertRowsToObjects(policyRows);
    
    // ì²« ë²ˆì§¸ ì •ì±…ì˜ í‚¤ë“¤ ì¶œë ¥ (ë§¤í•‘ í™•ì¸ìš©)
    if (policies.length > 0) {
      console.log('ğŸ“‹ ë³€í™˜ëœ ì²« ë²ˆì§¸ ì •ì±…ì˜ í‚¤ë“¤:', Object.keys(policies[0]));
      console.log('ğŸ“‹ applicationUrl ê°’:', policies[0].applicationUrl);
    }
    
    const policies = convertRowsToObjects(policyRows);
    
    // ìƒí™© ë°ì´í„° ê°€ì ¸ì˜¤ê¸° (ì„ íƒì‚¬í•­)
    let situations = [];
    try {
      const situationRows = await fetchSheetData(sheetId, 'ìƒí™©ë°ì´í„°!A:Z', apiKey);
      situations = convertRowsToObjects(situationRows);
    } catch (error) {
      console.warn('ìƒí™© ë°ì´í„° ì‹œíŠ¸ë¥¼ ì°¾ì„ ìˆ˜ ì—†ìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤. ê¸°ì¡´ ë°ì´í„°ë¥¼ ìœ ì§€í•©ë‹ˆë‹¤.');
      // ê¸°ì¡´ situations.json íŒŒì¼ ìœ ì§€
      if (fs.existsSync('src/data/situations.json')) {
        const existingData = JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync('src/data/situations.json', 'utf8'));
        situations = existingData.situations || [];
      }
    }
    
    // ë°ì´í„° ê²€ì¦
    const errors = validatePolicyData(policies);
    if (errors.length > 0) {
      console.error('âŒ ë°ì´í„° ê²€ì¦ ì‹¤íŒ¨:');
      errors.forEach(error => console.error(`  - ${error}`));
      process.exit(1);
    }
    
    // JSON íŒŒì¼ ìƒì„±
    const policiesData = { policies };
    const situationsData = { situations };
    
    fs.writeFileSync('src/data/policies.json', JSON.stringify(policiesData, null, 2));
    if (situations.length > 0) {
      fs.writeFileSync('src/data/situations.json', JSON.stringify(situationsData, null, 2));
    }
    
    console.log(`âœ… ì„±ê³µì ìœ¼ë¡œ ì—…ë°ì´íŠ¸ë˜ì—ˆìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤:`);
    console.log(`  - ì •ì±… ë°ì´í„°: ${policies.length}ê°œ`);
    console.log(`  - ìƒí™© ë°ì´í„°: ${situations.length}ê°œ`);
    
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('âŒ ì—…ë°ì´íŠ¸ ì‹¤íŒ¨:', error.message);
    process.exit(1);
  }
}
```

ì¤‘ë³µëœ ì¤„ì„ ì œê±°í•˜ê² ìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤:

```javascript
const fs = require('fs');
const axios = require('axios');

// Google Sheets APIë¥¼ í†µí•´ ë°ì´í„° ê°€ì ¸ì˜¤ê¸°
async function fetchSheetData(sheetId, range, apiKey) {
  const url = `https://sheets.googleapis.com/v4/spreadsheets/${sheetId}/values/${range}?key=${apiKey}`;
  
  try {
    const response = await axios.get(url);
    return response.data.values;
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('ì‹œíŠ¸ ë°ì´í„° ê°€ì ¸ì˜¤ê¸° ì‹¤íŒ¨:', error.message);
    throw error;
  }
}

// ë°°ì—´ ë°ì´í„°ë¥¼ JSON ê°ì²´ë¡œ ë³€í™˜
function convertRowsToObjects(rows) {
  if (!rows || rows.length < 2) return [];
  
  const headers = rows[0];
  const dataRows = rows.slice(1);
  
  return dataRows.map(row => {
    const obj = {};
    headers.forEach((header, index) => {
      let value = row[index] || '';
      
      // í—¤ë”ëª… ì •ê·œí™” (ëŒ€ë¬¸ì -> ì†Œë¬¸ì, íŠ¹ìˆ˜ ì¼€ì´ìŠ¤ ì²˜ë¦¬)
      let normalizedHeader = header.toLowerCase();
      
      // applicationUrl ë§¤í•‘ (ì˜¤íƒ€ ì¼€ì´ìŠ¤ í¬í•¨)
      if (normalizedHeader === 'applicationurl' || normalizedHeader === 'appicationurl') {
        normalizedHeader = 'applicationUrl';
      }
      if (normalizedHeader === 'createdat') {
        normalizedHeader = 'createdAt';
      }
      if (normalizedHeader === 'updatedat') {
        normalizedHeader = 'updatedAt';
      }
      if (normalizedHeader === 'detaileddescription') {
        normalizedHeader = 'detailedDescription';
      }
      
      // íŠ¹ë³„ ì²˜ë¦¬ê°€ í•„ìš”í•œ í•„ë“œë“¤
      if (normalizedHeader === 'situations' || normalizedHeader === 'tags') {
        // ì½¤ë§ˆë¡œ êµ¬ë¶„ëœ ë¬¸ìì—´ì„ ë°°ì—´ë¡œ ë³€í™˜
        value = value.split(',').map(item => item.trim()).filter(item => item);
      } else if (normalizedHeader === 'views') {
        // ìˆ«ì ë³€í™˜
        value = parseInt(value) || 0;
      } else if (normalizedHeader === 'deadline') {
        // ë‚ ì§œ í˜•ì‹ ê²€ì¦ (YYYY-MM-DD)
        if (value && !value.match(/^\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2}$/)) {
          console.warn(`ì˜ëª»ëœ ë‚ ì§œ í˜•ì‹: ${value}`);
        }
      }
      
      // ì •ê·œí™”ëœ í—¤ë”ëª…ìœ¼ë¡œ ì €ì¥
      obj[normalizedHeader] = value;
    });
    return obj;
  });
}

// ë°ì´í„° ê²€ì¦
function validatePolicyData(policies) {
  // í˜„ì¬ ìŠ¤í”„ë ˆë“œì‹œíŠ¸ì— ìˆëŠ” í•„ìˆ˜ í•„ë“œë“¤ë§Œ ì²´í¬
  const requiredFields = ['id', 'title', 'summary', 'category', 'source', 'tags', 'situations', 'target', 'amount', 'deadline', 'applicationUrl'];
  const errors = [];
  
  policies.forEach((policy, index) => {
    requiredFields.forEach(field => {
      if (!policy[field]) {
        errors.push(`ì •ì±… ${index + 1}: ${field} í•„ë“œê°€ ë¹„ì–´ìˆìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤.`);
      }
    });
    
    // URL í˜•ì‹ ê²€ì¦
    if (policy.applicationUrl && !policy.applicationUrl.startsWith('http')) {
      errors.push(`ì •ì±… ${index + 1}: applicationUrlì´ ì˜¬ë°”ë¥¸ URL í˜•ì‹ì´ ì•„ë‹™ë‹ˆë‹¤.`);
    }
    
    // ì¹´í…Œê³ ë¦¬ ê²€ì¦
    const validCategories = ['housing', 'employment-education', 'welfare', 'finance-startup', 'medical'];
    if (policy.category && !validCategories.includes(policy.category)) {
      errors.push(`ì •ì±… ${index + 1}: ìœ íš¨í•˜ì§€ ì•Šì€ ì¹´í…Œê³ ë¦¬ì…ë‹ˆë‹¤. (${policy.category})`);
    }
  });
  
  return errors;
}

async function main() {
  const apiKey = process.env.SHEETS_API_KEY;
  const sheetId = process.env.SHEETS_ID;
  
  if (!apiKey || !sheetId) {
    throw new Error('GOOGLE_SHEETS_API_KEY ë˜ëŠ” GOOGLE_SHEETS_ID í™˜ê²½ë³€ìˆ˜ê°€ ì„¤ì •ë˜ì§€ ì•Šì•˜ìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤.');
  }
  
  try {
    console.log('ğŸ“Š Google Sheetsì—ì„œ ì •ì±… ë°ì´í„°ë¥¼ ê°€ì ¸ì˜¤ëŠ” ì¤‘...');
    
    // ì •ì±… ë°ì´í„° ê°€ì ¸ì˜¤ê¸°
    const policyRows = await fetchSheetData(sheetId, 'ì •ì±…_ë§ˆìŠ¤í„°!A:Z', apiKey);
    
    // ë””ë²„ê¹…: í—¤ë”ì™€ ì²« ëª‡ í–‰ ì¶œë ¥
    console.log('ğŸ“‹ ìŠ¤í”„ë ˆë“œì‹œíŠ¸ í—¤ë”:', policyRows[0]);
    console.log('ğŸ“‹ ë°ì´í„° í–‰ ìˆ˜:', policyRows.length);
    if (policyRows.length > 1) {
      console.log('ğŸ“‹ ì²« ë²ˆì§¸ ë°ì´í„° í–‰:', policyRows[1]);
    }
    
    const policies = convertRowsToObjects(policyRows);
    
    // ì²« ë²ˆì§¸ ì •ì±…ì˜ í‚¤ë“¤ ì¶œë ¥ (ë§¤í•‘ í™•ì¸ìš©)
    if (policies.length > 0) {
      console.log('ğŸ“‹ ë³€í™˜ëœ ì²« ë²ˆì§¸ ì •ì±…ì˜ í‚¤ë“¤:', Object.keys(policies[0]));
      console.log('ğŸ“‹ applicationUrl ê°’:', policies[0].applicationUrl);
    }
    
    // ìƒí™© ë°ì´í„° ê°€ì ¸ì˜¤ê¸° (ì„ íƒì‚¬í•­)
    let situations = [];
    try {
      const situationRows = await fetchSheetData(sheetId, 'ìƒí™©ë°ì´í„°!A:Z', apiKey);
      situations = convertRowsToObjects(situationRows);
    } catch (error) {
      console.warn('ìƒí™© ë°ì´í„° ì‹œíŠ¸ë¥¼ ì°¾ì„ ìˆ˜ ì—†ìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤. ê¸°ì¡´ ë°ì´í„°ë¥¼ ìœ ì§€í•©ë‹ˆë‹¤.');
      // ê¸°ì¡´ situations.json íŒŒì¼ ìœ ì§€
      if (fs.existsSync('src/data/situations.json')) {
        const existingData = JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync('src/data/situations.json', 'utf8'));
        situations = existingData.situations || [];
      }
    }
    
    // ë°ì´í„° ê²€ì¦
    const errors = validatePolicyData(policies);
    if (errors.length > 0) {
      console.error('âŒ ë°ì´í„° ê²€ì¦ ì‹¤íŒ¨:');
      errors.forEach(error => console.error(`  - ${error}`));
      process.exit(1);
    }
    
    // JSON íŒŒì¼ ìƒì„±
    const policiesData = { policies };
    const situationsData = { situations };
    
    fs.writeFileSync('src/data/policies.json', JSON.stringify(policiesData, null, 2));
    if (situations.length > 0) {
      fs.writeFileSync('src/data/situations.json', JSON.stringify(situationsData, null, 2));
    }
    
    console.log(`âœ… ì„±ê³µì ìœ¼ë¡œ ì—…ë°ì´íŠ¸ë˜ì—ˆìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤:`);
    console.log(`  - ì •ì±… ë°ì´í„°: ${policies.length}ê°œ`);
    console.log(`  - ìƒí™© ë°ì´í„°: ${situations.length}ê°œ`);
    
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('âŒ ì—…ë°ì´íŠ¸ ì‹¤íŒ¨:', error.message);
    process.exit(1);
  }
}

main();
```

## ğŸ”§ **í•´ê²° ë°©ë²•: GitHub Actions ê¶Œí•œ ì„¤ì •**

### **1ë‹¨ê³„: GitHub ì €ì¥ì†Œ ì„¤ì • í™•ì¸**
1. **GitHub ì €ì¥ì†Œ â†’ Settings â†’ Actions â†’ General**
2. **"Workflow permissions" ì„¹ì…˜ì—ì„œ:**
   - âœ… **"Read and write permissions"** ì„ íƒ
   - âœ… **"Allow GitHub Actions to create and approve pull requests"** ì²´í¬

### **2ë‹¨ê³„: ì›Œí¬í”Œë¡œìš° íŒŒì¼ ê¶Œí•œ ì¶”ê°€**

```plaintext
Permission to gokimsk/polyfit.git denied to github-actions[bot]
fatal: unable to access 'https://github.com/gokimsk/polyfit/': The requested URL returned error: 403
```

```github-actions-workflow
name: Update Policies from Google Sheets

on:
  schedule:
    # ë§¤ì¼ ì˜¤ì „ 9ì‹œì— ìë™ ì‹¤í–‰ (KST ê¸°ì¤€)
    - cron: '0 0 * * *'
  workflow_dispatch:
    # ìˆ˜ë™ ì‹¤í–‰ ê°€ëŠ¥

jobs:
  update-data:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    permissions:
      contents: write
    
    steps:
    - name: Checkout repository
      uses: actions/checkout@v4
      
    - name: Setup Node.js
      uses: actions/setup-node@v4
      with:
        node-version: '18'
        
    - name: Install dependencies
      run: |
        npm install axios csv-parser
        
    - name: Download and convert Google Sheets data
      env:
        SHEETS_API_KEY: ${{ secrets.GOOGLE_SHEETS_API_KEY }}
        SHEETS_ID: ${{ secrets.GOOGLE_SHEETS_ID }}
      run: |
        node scripts/update-policies.js
        
    - name: Commit and push if changes
      run: |
        git config --local user.email "action@github.com"
        git config --local user.name "GitHub Action"
        git add src/data/
        
        if git diff --staged --quiet; then
          echo "No changes to commit"
        else
          git commit -m "ğŸ“Š ì •ì±… ë°ì´í„° ìë™ ì—…ë°ì´íŠ¸ $(date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M')"
          git push
        fi

```

## ğŸ¯ **ì¶”ê°€ í™•ì¸ì‚¬í•­: GitHub ì €ì¥ì†Œ ì„¤ì •**

1. **ì €ì¥ì†Œ â†’ Settings â†’ Actions â†’ General**
2. **"Workflow permissions" ì„¹ì…˜:**
   - **"Read and write permissions"** ì„ íƒ âœ…
   - **"Allow GitHub Actions to create and approve pull requests"** ì²´í¬ âœ…

3. **"Actions permissions" ì„¹ì…˜:**
   - **"Allow all actions and reusable workflows"** ì„ íƒ âœ…

```github-actions-workflow
    - name: Download and convert Google Sheets data
      env:
        SHEETS_API_KEY: ${{ secrets.GOOGLE_SHEETS_API_KEY }}
        SHEETS_ID: ${{ secrets.GOOGLE_SHEETS_ID }}
      run: |
        node scripts/update-policies.js
        
    - name: Commit and push if changes
      run: |
        git config --local user.email "action@github.com"
        git config --local user.name "GitHub Action"
        
        # ìµœì‹  ë³€ê²½ì‚¬í•­ ê°€ì ¸ì˜¤ê¸°
        git pull origin main
        
        git add src/data/
        
        if git diff --staged --quiet; then
          echo "No changes to commit"
        else
          git commit -m "ğŸ“Š ì •ì±… ë°ì´í„° ìë™ ì—…ë°ì´íŠ¸ $(date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M')"
          git push origin main
        fi

```

## ğŸ’¡ **ì¶”ì²œ í•´ê²°ì±…**

## ğŸ” **ì›ì¸ ë¶„ì„ ê²€í†  - ì •í™•í•©ë‹ˆë‹¤**

### âœ… **ì˜¬ë°”ë¥¸ ì§„ë‹¨:**
1. **shallow clone ë¬¸ì œ**: `checkout@v4`ê°€ ìµœì‹  ì»¤ë°‹ë§Œ ê°€ì ¸ì™€ì„œ Git íˆìŠ¤í† ë¦¬ ë¶ˆì™„ì „
2. **ìºì‹œëœ ì›Œí¬í”Œë¡œìš°**: ìš°ë¦¬ê°€ ìˆ˜ì •í•œ ì½”ë“œê°€ ì•„ì§ ë°˜ì˜ë˜ì§€ ì•ŠìŒ

## ğŸ› ï¸ **ì œì•ˆëœ í•´ê²°ë°©ì•ˆ í‰ê°€**

### **ë°©ì•ˆ 1: ìˆ˜ë™ ì¬ì‹œë„ ë¡œì§**
- **ì¥ì **: ìƒì„¸í•œ ë¡œê·¸, ì™„ì „í•œ ì œì–´
- **ë‹¨ì **: ë³µì¡í•¨, ìœ ì§€ë³´ìˆ˜ ì–´ë ¤ì›€

### **ë°©ì•ˆ 2: stefanzweifel/git-auto-commit-action (ê°•ë ¥ ì¶”ì²œ)**
- **ì¥ì **: ê²€ì¦ëœ ì†”ë£¨ì…˜, ì´ëŸ° ë¬¸ì œë“¤ì„ ì´ë¯¸ í•´ê²°í•¨
- **ë‹¨ì **: ì™¸ë¶€ ì˜ì¡´ì„±

## ğŸ’¡ **ìµœì¢… ì¶”ì²œ: ë°©ì•ˆ 2**

`stefanzweifel/git-auto-commit-action`ì´ ìµœì ì˜ ì„ íƒì¸ ì´ìœ :
1. **ì´ë¯¸ ê²€ì¦ë¨**: ìˆ˜ì²œ ê°œ í”„ë¡œì íŠ¸ì—ì„œ ì‚¬ìš© ì¤‘
2. **ì¶©ëŒ ì²˜ë¦¬**: ìë™ìœ¼ë¡œ fetch, rebase, retry ì²˜ë¦¬
3. **ê°„ë‹¨í•¨**: ë³µì¡í•œ ìŠ¤í¬ë¦½íŠ¸ ë¶ˆí•„ìš”
4. **ì•ˆì •ì„±**: Edge caseë“¤ì„ ëª¨ë‘ ê³ ë ¤í•´ì„œ ê°œë°œë¨

## ğŸš€ **ì‹¤í–‰ ê³„íš**

```github-actions-workflow
name: Update Policies from Google Sheets

on:
  schedule:
    # ë§¤ì¼ ì˜¤ì „ 9ì‹œì— ìë™ ì‹¤í–‰ (KST ê¸°ì¤€)
    - cron: '0 0 * * *'
  workflow_dispatch:
    # ìˆ˜ë™ ì‹¤í–‰ ê°€ëŠ¥

jobs:
  update-data:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    permissions:
      contents: write
    
    steps:
    - name: Checkout repository
      uses: actions/checkout@v4
      with:
        fetch-depth: 0
        token: ${{ secrets.GITHUB_TOKEN }}
      
    - name: Setup Node.js
      uses: actions/setup-node@v4
      with:
        node-version: '18'
        
    - name: Install dependencies
      run: |
        npm install axios csv-parser
        
    - name: Download and convert Google Sheets data
      env:
        SHEETS_API_KEY: ${{ secrets.GOOGLE_SHEETS_API_KEY }}
        SHEETS_ID: ${{ secrets.GOOGLE_SHEETS_ID }}
      run: |
        node scripts/update-policies.js
        
    - name: Commit and push if changes
      run: |
        git config --local user.email "action@github.com"
        git config --local user.name "GitHub Action"
        
        git add src/data/
        
        if git diff --staged --quiet; then
          echo "No changes to commit"
        else
          git commit -m "ğŸ“Š ì •ì±… ë°ì´í„° ìë™ ì—…ë°ì´íŠ¸ $(date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M')"
          
          # pullê³¼ pushë¥¼ ë°˜ë³µí•´ì„œ ì‹œë„ (ìµœëŒ€ 3ë²ˆ)
          for i in {1..3}; do
            echo "Push attempt $i"
            git pull --rebase origin main && git push origin main && break
            if [ $i -eq 3 ]; then
              echo "Failed to push after 3 attempts"
              exit 1
            fi
            sleep 5
          done
        fi

```

```github-actions-workflow
    - name: Commit and push if changes
      uses: stefanzweifel/git-auto-commit-action@v5
      with:
        commit_message: 'ğŸ“Š ì •ì±… ë°ì´í„° ìë™ ì—…ë°ì´íŠ¸'
        file_pattern: 'src/data/*'
        commit_user_name: 'github-actions[bot]'
        commit_user_email: 'github-actions[bot]@users.noreply.github.com'
```

íŒŒì¼ì„ ë‹¤ì‹œ ì½ì–´ì„œ ì •í™•í•œ ë‚´ìš©ì„ í™•ì¸í•˜ê² ìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤:

ì•„, ì´ë¯¸ ì¬ì‹œë„ ë¡œì§ì´ ì¶”ê°€ë˜ì–´ ìˆì—ˆë„¤ìš”. ì´ë¥¼ ê²€ì¦ëœ ì•¡ì…˜ìœ¼ë¡œ êµì²´í•˜ê² ìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤:

```typescriptreact
import { loadPolicies } from '@/lib/utils';
import { calculateMatchScore } from '@/lib/matching';

// í•˜ë“œì½”ë”©ëœ ìƒí™© íƒœê·¸ (ë§¤ì¹­ ë¡œì§ì—ì„œ ì‚¬ìš©)
const SITUATION_TAGS: Record<SituationId, string[]> = {
  independence: ['ìì·¨', 'ë…ë¦½', 'ìƒí™œë¹„', 'ì£¼ê±°ë¹„', 'ê°€êµ¬', 'ìƒí™œìš©í’ˆ'],
  'job-seeking': ['êµ¬ì§', 'ì·¨ì—…', 'ì´ë ¥ì„œ', 'ë©´ì ‘', 'êµìœ¡', 'í›ˆë ¨'],
  'after-resignation': ['í‡´ì‚¬', 'ì „ì§', 'ì°½ì—…', 'êµìœ¡', 'ìê²©ì¦', 'ì¬ì·¨ì—…'],
  'childcare-prep': ['ìœ¡ì•„', 'ì„ì‹ ', 'ì¶œì‚°', 'ë³´ìœ¡', 'êµìœ¡', 'ë³µì§€'],
  'tax-settlement': ['ì—°ë§ì •ì‚°', 'ì„¸ê¸ˆ', 'í™˜ê¸‰', 'ê³µì œ', 'ì‹ ê³ ', 'ì ˆì„¸'],
  'marriage-prep': ['ê²°í˜¼', 'ì‹ í˜¼', 'í˜¼ë¡€', 'ì‹ í˜¼ë¶€ë¶€', 'ì£¼íƒ', 'ëŒ€ì¶œ']
};

const SITUATION_LABELS = {
  independence: 'ìì·¨ ì‹œì‘',
  'job-seeking': 'êµ¬ì§ ì¤‘',
  'after-resignation': 'í‡´ì‚¬ í›„',
  'childcare-prep': 'ìœ¡ì•„ ì¤€ë¹„',
  'tax-settlement': 'ì—°ë§ì •ì‚°',
  'marriage-prep': 'ê²°í˜¼ ì¤€ë¹„'
};

export default function DebugPage() {
  const [policies, setPolicies] = useState<Policy[]>([]);
  const [selectedSituations, setSelectedSituations] = useState<SituationId[]>(['independence']);
  const [debugResults, setDebugResults] = useState<any[]>([]);

  useEffect(() => {
    const allPolicies = loadPolicies();
    setPolicies(allPolicies);
  }, []);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (policies.length > 0) {
      runDebugTest();
    }
  }, [policies, selectedSituations]);

  const runDebugTest = () => {
    // ì„ íƒëœ ìƒí™©ë“¤ì˜ íƒœê·¸ í•©ì¹˜ê¸°
    const selectedTags = new Set<string>();
    selectedSituations.forEach(situationId => {
      SITUATION_TAGS[situationId].forEach(tag => selectedTags.add(tag));
    });

    const results = policies.map(policy => {
      const score = calculateMatchScore(selectedSituations, policy);
      
      // íƒœê·¸ ë§¤ì¹­ ë¶„ì„
      const tagMatches = policy.tags.filter(tag => selectedTags.has(tag));
      const tagScore = tagMatches.length * 10;

      // ìƒí™© ë§¤ì¹­ ë¶„ì„  
      const situationMatches = policy.situations.filter(situation => 
        selectedSituations.includes(situation)
      );
      const situationScore = situationMatches.length * 5;

      // ë§ˆê° ì„ë°• ë³´ë„ˆìŠ¤
      const today = new Date();
      const deadline = new Date(policy.deadline);
      const daysUntilDeadline = Math.ceil((deadline.getTime() - today.getTime()) / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24));
      const deadlineBonus = (daysUntilDeadline <= 30 && daysUntilDeadline > 0) ? 1 : 0;

      return {
        policy,
        totalScore: score,
        breakdown: {
          tagMatches,
          tagScore,
          situationMatches,
          situationScore,
          deadlineBonus,
          daysUntilDeadline
        }
      };
    }).sort((a, b) => b.totalScore - a.totalScore);

    setDebugResults(results);
  };

  const toggleSituation = (situationId: SituationId) => {
    setSelectedSituations(prev => {
      if (prev.includes(situationId)) {
        return prev.filter(id => id !== situationId);
      } else {
        return [...prev, situationId];
      }
    });
  };

  const selectedTagsArray = Array.from(
    new Set(selectedSituations.flatMap(id => SITUATION_TAGS[id]))
  );

  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen bg-gray-50 p-8">
      <div className="max-w-6xl mx-auto">
        <h1 className="text-3xl font-bold text-gray-900 mb-8">ğŸ” ë§¤ì¹­ ì•Œê³ ë¦¬ì¦˜ ë””ë²„ê¹…</h1>
        
        {/* ìƒí™© ì„ íƒê¸° */}
        <div className="bg-white rounded-lg p-6 mb-8 shadow">
          <h2 className="text-xl font-semibold mb-4">í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸í•  ìƒí™© ì„ íƒ</h2>
          <div className="grid grid-cols-2 md:grid-cols-3 gap-4">
            {Object.entries(SITUATION_LABELS).map(([id, label]) => (
              <button
                key={id}
                onClick={() => toggleSituation(id as SituationId)}
                className={`p-3 rounded-lg border-2 text-left transition-colors ${
                  selectedSituations.includes(id as SituationId)
                    ? 'border-blue-500 bg-blue-50 text-blue-700'
                    : 'border-gray-200 hover:border-gray-300'
                }`}
              >
                <div className="font-medium">{label}</div>
                <div className="text-sm text-gray-500">{id}</div>
              </button>
            ))}
          </div>

          {/* ì„ íƒëœ íƒœê·¸ í‘œì‹œ */}
          <div className="mt-4">
            <h3 className="font-medium text-gray-700 mb-2">ì„ íƒëœ ìƒí™©ì˜ íƒœê·¸ë“¤:</h3>
            <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-2">
              {selectedTagsArray.map(tag => (
                <span key={tag} className="px-2 py-1 bg-blue-100 text-blue-700 rounded text-sm">
                  {tag}
                </span>
              ))}
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>

        {/* ë””ë²„ê¹… ê²°ê³¼ */}
        <div className="space-y-4">
          <h2 className="text-xl font-semibold">ë§¤ì¹­ ê²°ê³¼ (ì´ {debugResults.length}ê°œ ì •ì±…)</h2>
          
          {debugResults.map(({ policy, totalScore, breakdown }, index) => (
            <div key={policy.id} className="bg-white rounded-lg p-6 shadow">
              <div className="flex justify-between items-start mb-4">
                <div>
                  <h3 className="text-lg font-semibold text-gray-900">{policy.title}</h3>
                  <p className="text-sm text-gray-600">{policy.id} | {policy.category}</p>
                </div>
                <div className="text-right">
                  <div className="text-2xl font-bold text-blue-600">{totalScore}ì </div>
                  <div className="text-sm text-gray-500">#{index + 1}</div>
                </div>
              </div>

              {/* ì ìˆ˜ ë¶„ì„ */}
              <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-3 gap-4 mb-4">
                <div className="bg-green-50 p-3 rounded">
                  <div className="font-medium text-green-800">íƒœê·¸ ë§¤ì¹­</div>
                  <div className="text-green-600">{breakdown.tagScore}ì  ({breakdown.tagMatches.length}ê°œ ë§¤ì¹­)</div>
                  <div className="text-xs text-green-600 mt-1">
                    {breakdown.tagMatches.join(', ') || 'ë§¤ì¹­ ì—†ìŒ'}
                  </div>
                </div>

                <div className="bg-blue-50 p-3 rounded">
                  <div className="font-medium text-blue-800">ìƒí™© ë§¤ì¹­</div>
                  <div className="text-blue-600">{breakdown.situationScore}ì  ({breakdown.situationMatches.length}ê°œ ë§¤ì¹­)</div>
                  <div className="text-xs text-blue-600 mt-1">
                    {breakdown.situationMatches.join(', ') || 'ë§¤ì¹­ ì—†ìŒ'}
                  </div>
                </div>

                <div className="bg-orange-50 p-3 rounded">
                  <div className="font-medium text-orange-800">ë§ˆê° ë³´ë„ˆìŠ¤</div>
                  <div className="text-orange-600">{breakdown.deadlineBonus}ì </div>
                  <div className="text-xs text-orange-600 mt-1">
                    {breakdown.daysUntilDeadline}ì¼ ë‚¨ìŒ
                  </div>
                </div>
              </div>

              {/* ì •ì±… íƒœê·¸ */}
              <div>
                <div className="font-medium text-gray-700 mb-2">ì •ì±… íƒœê·¸:</div>
                <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-2">
                  {policy.tags.map(tag => {
                    const isMatched = selectedTagsArray.includes(tag);
                    return (
                      <span 
                        key={tag} 
                        className={`px-2 py-1 rounded text-sm ${
                          isMatched 
                            ? 'bg-green-100 text-green-700 font-medium' 
                            : 'bg-gray-100 text-gray-600'
                        }`}
                      >
                        {tag}
                      </span>
                    );
                  })}
                </div>
              </div>
            </div>
          ))}
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}
```

## âœ… **ë””ë²„ê¹… ë„êµ¬ ë°°í¬ ì™„ë£Œ!**

## ğŸ“‹ **ë””ë²„ê¹… í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ ì§„í–‰ ë°©ë²•**

### **2ë‹¨ê³„: ì²´ê³„ì  í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ ì‹¤í–‰**

#### **í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ ì¼€ì´ìŠ¤ 1: ë‹¨ì¼ ìƒí™© ì„ íƒ**
1. **ìì·¨ ì‹œì‘ë§Œ** ì„ íƒ
2. **ì˜ˆìƒ ê²°ê³¼**: ì£¼ê±° ê´€ë ¨ ì •ì±…ì´ ë†’ì€ ì ìˆ˜
3. **í™•ì¸ ì‚¬í•­**: 
   - `["ì£¼ê±°", "ì²­ë…„", "ì›”ì„¸", "ìƒí™œë¹„", "ë…ë¦½", "ë³´ì¦ê¸ˆ"]` íƒœê·¸ë¥¼ ê°€ì§„ ì •ì±…
   - `ìƒí™œë¹„`, `ë…ë¦½` ë§¤ì¹­ìœ¼ë¡œ 20ì 

#### **í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ ì¼€ì´ìŠ¤ 2: ë³µí•© ìƒí™© ì„ íƒ**  
1. **ìì·¨ ì‹œì‘ + êµ¬ì§ ì¤‘** ì„ íƒ
2. **ì˜ˆìƒ ê²°ê³¼**: ì·¨ì—…+ì£¼ê±° ì •ì±…ì´ ìµœìƒìœ„
3. **í™•ì¸ ì‚¬í•­**: íƒœê·¸ ì¤‘ë³µ ì œê±° ë° ì ìˆ˜ ê°€ì‚°

#### **í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ ì¼€ì´ìŠ¤ 3: ì‹¤ì œ ìŠ¤í”„ë ˆë“œì‹œíŠ¸ ë°ì´í„° ê²€ì¦**
1. ê° ì •ì±…ì˜ `tags` í•„ë“œê°€ ë°°ì—´ë¡œ ì˜¬ë°”ë¥´ê²Œ íŒŒì‹±ë˜ëŠ”ì§€
2. `situations` í•„ë“œê°€ ì˜¬ë°”ë¥´ê²Œ ë§¤ì¹­ë˜ëŠ”ì§€

**ì˜ˆìƒ ê°€ëŠ¥í•œ ë¬¸ì œë“¤:**
- â“ ìŠ¤í”„ë ˆë“œì‹œíŠ¸ íƒœê·¸ vs í•˜ë“œì½”ë”© íƒœê·¸ ë¶ˆì¼ì¹˜
- â“ JSON íŒŒì‹± í›„ ë°°ì—´ í˜•íƒœ í™•ì¸ í•„ìš”
- â“ í•œê¸€ íƒœê·¸ ë§¤ì¹­ ì •í™•ë„

## ğŸ¯ **ì§€ê¸ˆ í•´ì•¼ í•  ì¼**

1. **ë°°í¬ëœ ì‚¬ì´íŠ¸ì˜ `/debug` í˜ì´ì§€ ì ‘ì†**
2. **ê° í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ ì¼€ì´ìŠ¤ ì‹¤í–‰**
3. **ë§¤ì¹­ ì ìˆ˜ì™€ íƒœê·¸ ë¶„ì„ ê²°ê³¼ í™•ì¸**
4. **ë¬¸ì œì  ë°œê²¬ì‹œ ë³´ê³ **

**ë””ë²„ê¹… í˜ì´ì§€ì— ì ‘ì†í•´ì„œ ì‹¤ì œ ë§¤ì¹­ ë™ì‘ì„ í™•ì¸í•´ë³´ì‹œê³ , ì–´ë–¤ ë¬¸ì œì ì´ ë°œê²¬ë˜ëŠ”ì§€ ì•Œë ¤ì£¼ì„¸ìš”!** ğŸ”

ë°œê²¬ëœ ì´ìŠˆì— ë”°ë¼ ë§¤ì¹­ ë¡œì§ì´ë‚˜ ë°ì´í„° êµ¬ì¡°ë¥¼ ê°œì„ í•˜ê² ìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤.

**User**

ì–´ë–¤ ìƒí™©ì„ ì„ íƒí•´ë„ ë§¤ì¹­ê²°ê³¼ê°€ 0ì ì´ì•¼ 

---

**Cursor**

ë§¤ì¹­ ì ìˆ˜ê°€ ëª¨ë‘ 0ì ì¸ ë¬¸ì œë¥¼ í™•ì¸í•´ë³´ê² ìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤. ì´ëŠ” ë°ì´í„° êµ¬ì¡° ë¶ˆì¼ì¹˜ ë•Œë¬¸ì¼ ê°€ëŠ¥ì„±ì´ ë†’ìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤.

ğŸ” **ë¬¸ì œ ë°œê²¬!** 

íƒœê·¸ì™€ ìƒí™© ë°ì´í„°ê°€ **ì´ì¤‘ìœ¼ë¡œ JSON ì¸ì½”ë”©**ë˜ì–´ ìˆìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤:

- **í˜„ì¬ ìƒíƒœ**: `["[\"ì£¼ê±°\"", "\"ì²­ë…„\"", "\"ì›”ì„¸\"", ...]`
- **ì˜ˆìƒ ìƒíƒœ**: `["ì£¼ê±°", "ì²­ë…„", "ì›”ì„¸", ...]`

## ğŸ”§ **í•´ê²° ë°©ë²•: ë°ì´í„° ë³€í™˜ ìŠ¤í¬ë¦½íŠ¸ ìˆ˜ì •**

```javascript
const fs = require('fs');
const axios = require('axios');

// Google Sheets APIë¥¼ í†µí•´ ë°ì´í„° ê°€ì ¸ì˜¤ê¸°
async function fetchSheetData(sheetId, range, apiKey) {
  const url = `https://sheets.googleapis.com/v4/spreadsheets/${sheetId}/values/${range}?key=${apiKey}`;
  
  try {
    const response = await axios.get(url);
    return response.data.values;
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('ì‹œíŠ¸ ë°ì´í„° ê°€ì ¸ì˜¤ê¸° ì‹¤íŒ¨:', error.message);
    throw error;
  }
}

// ë°°ì—´ ë°ì´í„°ë¥¼ JSON ê°ì²´ë¡œ ë³€í™˜
function convertRowsToObjects(rows) {
  if (!rows || rows.length < 2) return [];
  
  const headers = rows[0];
  const dataRows = rows.slice(1);
  
  return dataRows.map(row => {
    const obj = {};
    headers.forEach((header, index) => {
      let value = row[index] || '';
      
      // í—¤ë”ëª… ì •ê·œí™” (ëŒ€ë¬¸ì -> ì†Œë¬¸ì, íŠ¹ìˆ˜ ì¼€ì´ìŠ¤ ì²˜ë¦¬)
      let normalizedHeader = header.toLowerCase();
      
      // applicationUrl ë§¤í•‘ (ì˜¤íƒ€ ì¼€ì´ìŠ¤ í¬í•¨)
      if (normalizedHeader === 'applicationurl' || normalizedHeader === 'appicationurl') {
        normalizedHeader = 'applicationUrl';
      }
      if (normalizedHeader === 'createdat') {
        normalizedHeader = 'createdAt';
      }
      if (normalizedHeader === 'updatedat') {
        normalizedHeader = 'updatedAt';
      }
      if (normalizedHeader === 'detaileddescription') {
        normalizedHeader = 'detailedDescription';
      }
      
      // íŠ¹ë³„ ì²˜ë¦¬ê°€ í•„ìš”í•œ í•„ë“œë“¤
      if (normalizedHeader === 'situations' || normalizedHeader === 'tags') {
        // JSON ë¬¸ìì—´ì¸ ê²½ìš° íŒŒì‹±
        if (typeof value === 'string' && value.startsWith('[') && value.endsWith(']')) {
          try {
            value = JSON.parse(value);
          } catch (e) {
            console.warn(`JSON íŒŒì‹± ì‹¤íŒ¨ (${normalizedHeader}): ${value}`);
            // ì½¤ë§ˆë¡œ êµ¬ë¶„ëœ ë¬¸ìì—´ë¡œ í´ë°±
            value = value.split(',').map(item => item.trim()).filter(item => item);
          }
        } else {
          // ì½¤ë§ˆë¡œ êµ¬ë¶„ëœ ë¬¸ìì—´ì„ ë°°ì—´ë¡œ ë³€í™˜
          value = value.split(',').map(item => item.trim()).filter(item => item);
        }
      } else if (normalizedHeader === 'views') {
        // ìˆ«ì ë³€í™˜
        value = parseInt(value) || 0;
      } else if (normalizedHeader === 'deadline') {
        // ë‚ ì§œ í˜•ì‹ ê²€ì¦ (YYYY-MM-DD)
        if (value && !value.match(/^\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2}$/)) {
          console.warn(`ì˜ëª»ëœ ë‚ ì§œ í˜•ì‹: ${value}`);
        }
      }
      
      // ì •ê·œí™”ëœ í—¤ë”ëª…ìœ¼ë¡œ ì €ì¥
      obj[normalizedHeader] = value;
    });
    return obj;
  });
}

// ë°ì´í„° ê²€ì¦
function validatePolicyData(policies) {
  // í˜„ì¬ ìŠ¤í”„ë ˆë“œì‹œíŠ¸ì— ìˆëŠ” í•„ìˆ˜ í•„ë“œë“¤ë§Œ ì²´í¬
  const requiredFields = ['id', 'title', 'summary', 'category', 'source', 'tags', 'situations', 'target', 'amount', 'deadline', 'applicationUrl'];
  const errors = [];
  
  policies.forEach((policy, index) => {
    requiredFields.forEach(field => {
      if (!policy[field]) {
        errors.push(`ì •ì±… ${index + 1}: ${field} í•„ë“œê°€ ë¹„ì–´ìˆìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤.`);
      }
    });
    
    // URL í˜•ì‹ ê²€ì¦
    if (policy.applicationUrl && !policy.applicationUrl.startsWith('http')) {
      errors.push(`ì •ì±… ${index + 1}: applicationUrlì´ ì˜¬ë°”ë¥¸ URL í˜•ì‹ì´ ì•„ë‹™ë‹ˆë‹¤.`);
    }
    
    // ì¹´í…Œê³ ë¦¬ ê²€ì¦
    const validCategories = ['housing', 'employment-education', 'welfare', 'finance-startup', 'medical'];
    if (policy.category && !validCategories.includes(policy.category)) {
      errors.push(`ì •ì±… ${index + 1}: ìœ íš¨í•˜ì§€ ì•Šì€ ì¹´í…Œê³ ë¦¬ì…ë‹ˆë‹¤. (${policy.category})`);
    }
  });
  
  return errors;
}

async function main() {
  const apiKey = process.env.SHEETS_API_KEY;
  const sheetId = process.env.SHEETS_ID;
  
  if (!apiKey || !sheetId) {
    throw new Error('GOOGLE_SHEETS_API_KEY ë˜ëŠ” GOOGLE_SHEETS_ID í™˜ê²½ë³€ìˆ˜ê°€ ì„¤ì •ë˜ì§€ ì•Šì•˜ìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤.');
  }
  
  try {
    console.log('ğŸ“Š Google Sheetsì—ì„œ ì •ì±… ë°ì´í„°ë¥¼ ê°€ì ¸ì˜¤ëŠ” ì¤‘...');
    
    // ì •ì±… ë°ì´í„° ê°€ì ¸ì˜¤ê¸°
    const policyRows = await fetchSheetData(sheetId, 'ì •ì±…_ë§ˆìŠ¤í„°!A:Z', apiKey);
    
    // ë””ë²„ê¹…: í—¤ë”ì™€ ì²« ëª‡ í–‰ ì¶œë ¥
    console.log('ğŸ“‹ ìŠ¤í”„ë ˆë“œì‹œíŠ¸ í—¤ë”:', policyRows[0]);
    console.log('ğŸ“‹ ë°ì´í„° í–‰ ìˆ˜:', policyRows.length);
    if (policyRows.length > 1) {
      console.log('ğŸ“‹ ì²« ë²ˆì§¸ ë°ì´í„° í–‰:', policyRows[1]);
    }
    
    const policies = convertRowsToObjects(policyRows);
    
    // ì²« ë²ˆì§¸ ì •ì±…ì˜ í‚¤ë“¤ ì¶œë ¥ (ë§¤í•‘ í™•ì¸ìš©)
    if (policies.length > 0) {
      console.log('ğŸ“‹ ë³€í™˜ëœ ì²« ë²ˆì§¸ ì •ì±…ì˜ í‚¤ë“¤:', Object.keys(policies[0]));
      console.log('ğŸ“‹ applicationUrl ê°’:', policies[0].applicationUrl);
    }
    
    // ìƒí™© ë°ì´í„° ê°€ì ¸ì˜¤ê¸° (ì„ íƒì‚¬í•­)
    let situations = [];
    try {
      const situationRows = await fetchSheetData(sheetId, 'ìƒí™©ë°ì´í„°!A:Z', apiKey);
      situations = convertRowsToObjects(situationRows);
    } catch (error) {
      console.warn('ìƒí™© ë°ì´í„° ì‹œíŠ¸ë¥¼ ì°¾ì„ ìˆ˜ ì—†ìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤. ê¸°ì¡´ ë°ì´í„°ë¥¼ ìœ ì§€í•©ë‹ˆë‹¤.');
      // ê¸°ì¡´ situations.json íŒŒì¼ ìœ ì§€
      if (fs.existsSync('src/data/situations.json')) {
        const existingData = JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync('src/data/situations.json', 'utf8'));
        situations = existingData.situations || [];
      }
    }
    
    // ë°ì´í„° ê²€ì¦
    const errors = validatePolicyData(policies);
    if (errors.length > 0) {
      console.error('âŒ ë°ì´í„° ê²€ì¦ ì‹¤íŒ¨:');
      errors.forEach(error => console.error(`  - ${error}`));
      process.exit(1);
    }
    
    // JSON íŒŒì¼ ìƒì„±
    const policiesData = { policies };
    const situationsData = { situations };
    
    fs.writeFileSync('src/data/policies.json', JSON.stringify(policiesData, null, 2));
    if (situations.length > 0) {
      fs.writeFileSync('src/data/situations.json', JSON.stringify(situationsData, null, 2));
    }
    
    console.log(`âœ… ì„±ê³µì ìœ¼ë¡œ ì—…ë°ì´íŠ¸ë˜ì—ˆìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤:`);
    console.log(`  - ì •ì±… ë°ì´í„°: ${policies.length}ê°œ`);
    console.log(`  - ìƒí™© ë°ì´í„°: ${situations.length}ê°œ`);
    
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('âŒ ì—…ë°ì´íŠ¸ ì‹¤íŒ¨:', error.message);
    process.exit(1);
  }
}

main();

```

ë””ë²„ê¹… ë¡œê·¸ë„ ì¶”ê°€í•´ì„œ ë³€í™˜ ê³¼ì •ì„ í™•ì¸í•  ìˆ˜ ìˆê²Œ í•˜ê² ìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤:

```javascript
const fs = require('fs');
const axios = require('axios');

// Google Sheets APIë¥¼ í†µí•´ ë°ì´í„° ê°€ì ¸ì˜¤ê¸°
async function fetchSheetData(sheetId, range, apiKey) {
  const url = `https://sheets.googleapis.com/v4/spreadsheets/${sheetId}/values/${range}?key=${apiKey}`;
  
  try {
    const response = await axios.get(url);
    return response.data.values;
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('ì‹œíŠ¸ ë°ì´í„° ê°€ì ¸ì˜¤ê¸° ì‹¤íŒ¨:', error.message);
    throw error;
  }
}

// ë°°ì—´ ë°ì´í„°ë¥¼ JSON ê°ì²´ë¡œ ë³€í™˜
function convertRowsToObjects(rows) {
  if (!rows || rows.length < 2) return [];
  
  const headers = rows[0];
  const dataRows = rows.slice(1);
  
  return dataRows.map(row => {
    const obj = {};
    headers.forEach((header, index) => {
      let value = row[index] || '';
      
      // í—¤ë”ëª… ì •ê·œí™” (ëŒ€ë¬¸ì -> ì†Œë¬¸ì, íŠ¹ìˆ˜ ì¼€ì´ìŠ¤ ì²˜ë¦¬)
      let normalizedHeader = header.toLowerCase();
      
      // applicationUrl ë§¤í•‘ (ì˜¤íƒ€ ì¼€ì´ìŠ¤ í¬í•¨)
      if (normalizedHeader === 'applicationurl' || normalizedHeader === 'appicationurl') {
        normalizedHeader = 'applicationUrl';
      }
      if (normalizedHeader === 'createdat') {
        normalizedHeader = 'createdAt';
      }
      if (normalizedHeader === 'updatedat') {
        normalizedHeader = 'updatedAt';
      }
      if (normalizedHeader === 'detaileddescription') {
        normalizedHeader = 'detailedDescription';
      }
      
      // íŠ¹ë³„ ì²˜ë¦¬ê°€ í•„ìš”í•œ í•„ë“œë“¤
      if (normalizedHeader === 'situations' || normalizedHeader === 'tags') {
        // JSON ë¬¸ìì—´ì¸ ê²½ìš° íŒŒì‹±
        if (typeof value === 'string' && value.startsWith('[') && value.endsWith(']')) {
          try {
            value = JSON.parse(value);
          } catch (e) {
            console.warn(`JSON íŒŒì‹± ì‹¤íŒ¨ (${normalizedHeader}): ${value}`);
            // ì½¤ë§ˆë¡œ êµ¬ë¶„ëœ ë¬¸ìì—´ë¡œ í´ë°±
            value = value.split(',').map(item => item.trim()).filter(item => item);
          }
        } else {
          // ì½¤ë§ˆë¡œ êµ¬ë¶„ëœ ë¬¸ìì—´ì„ ë°°ì—´ë¡œ ë³€í™˜
          value = value.split(',').map(item => item.trim()).filter(item => item);
        }
      } else if (normalizedHeader === 'views') {
        // ìˆ«ì ë³€í™˜
        value = parseInt(value) || 0;
      } else if (normalizedHeader === 'deadline') {
        // ë‚ ì§œ í˜•ì‹ ê²€ì¦ (YYYY-MM-DD)
        if (value && !value.match(/^\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2}$/)) {
          console.warn(`ì˜ëª»ëœ ë‚ ì§œ í˜•ì‹: ${value}`);
        }
      }
      
      // ì •ê·œí™”ëœ í—¤ë”ëª…ìœ¼ë¡œ ì €ì¥
      obj[normalizedHeader] = value;
    });
    return obj;
  });
}

// ë°ì´í„° ê²€ì¦
function validatePolicyData(policies) {
  // í˜„ì¬ ìŠ¤í”„ë ˆë“œì‹œíŠ¸ì— ìˆëŠ” í•„ìˆ˜ í•„ë“œë“¤ë§Œ ì²´í¬
  const requiredFields = ['id', 'title', 'summary', 'category', 'source', 'tags', 'situations', 'target', 'amount', 'deadline', 'applicationUrl'];
  const errors = [];
  
  policies.forEach((policy, index) => {
    requiredFields.forEach(field => {
      if (!policy[field]) {
        errors.push(`ì •ì±… ${index + 1}: ${field} í•„ë“œê°€ ë¹„ì–´ìˆìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤.`);
      }
    });
    
    // URL í˜•ì‹ ê²€ì¦
    if (policy.applicationUrl && !policy.applicationUrl.startsWith('http')) {
      errors.push(`ì •ì±… ${index + 1}: applicationUrlì´ ì˜¬ë°”ë¥¸ URL í˜•ì‹ì´ ì•„ë‹™ë‹ˆë‹¤.`);
    }
    
    // ì¹´í…Œê³ ë¦¬ ê²€ì¦
    const validCategories = ['housing', 'employment-education', 'welfare', 'finance-startup', 'medical'];
    if (policy.category && !validCategories.includes(policy.category)) {
      errors.push(`ì •ì±… ${index + 1}: ìœ íš¨í•˜ì§€ ì•Šì€ ì¹´í…Œê³ ë¦¬ì…ë‹ˆë‹¤. (${policy.category})`);
    }
  });
  
  return errors;
}

async function main() {
  const apiKey = process.env.SHEETS_API_KEY;
  const sheetId = process.env.SHEETS_ID;
  
  if (!apiKey || !sheetId) {
    throw new Error('GOOGLE_SHEETS_API_KEY ë˜ëŠ” GOOGLE_SHEETS_ID í™˜ê²½ë³€ìˆ˜ê°€ ì„¤ì •ë˜ì§€ ì•Šì•˜ìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤.');
  }
  
  try {
    console.log('ğŸ“Š Google Sheetsì—ì„œ ì •ì±… ë°ì´í„°ë¥¼ ê°€ì ¸ì˜¤ëŠ” ì¤‘...');
    
    // ì •ì±… ë°ì´í„° ê°€ì ¸ì˜¤ê¸°
    const policyRows = await fetchSheetData(sheetId, 'ì •ì±…_ë§ˆìŠ¤í„°!A:Z', apiKey);
    
    // ë””ë²„ê¹…: í—¤ë”ì™€ ì²« ëª‡ í–‰ ì¶œë ¥
    console.log('ğŸ“‹ ìŠ¤í”„ë ˆë“œì‹œíŠ¸ í—¤ë”:', policyRows[0]);
    console.log('ğŸ“‹ ë°ì´í„° í–‰ ìˆ˜:', policyRows.length);
    if (policyRows.length > 1) {
      console.log('ğŸ“‹ ì²« ë²ˆì§¸ ë°ì´í„° í–‰:', policyRows[1]);
    }
    
    const policies = convertRowsToObjects(policyRows);
    
    // ì²« ë²ˆì§¸ ì •ì±…ì˜ í‚¤ë“¤ ì¶œë ¥ (ë§¤í•‘ í™•ì¸ìš©)
    if (policies.length > 0) {
      console.log('ğŸ“‹ ë³€í™˜ëœ ì²« ë²ˆì§¸ ì •ì±…ì˜ í‚¤ë“¤:', Object.keys(policies[0]));
      console.log('ğŸ“‹ applicationUrl ê°’:', policies[0].applicationUrl);
      console.log('ğŸ“‹ tags ê°’:', policies[0].tags);
      console.log('ğŸ“‹ situations ê°’:', policies[0].situations);
      console.log('ğŸ“‹ tags íƒ€ì…:', typeof policies[0].tags, Array.isArray(policies[0].tags));
      console.log('ğŸ“‹ situations íƒ€ì…:', typeof policies[0].situations, Array.isArray(policies[0].situations));
    }
    
    // ìƒí™© ë°ì´í„° ê°€ì ¸ì˜¤ê¸° (ì„ íƒì‚¬í•­)
    let situations = [];
    try {
      const situationRows = await fetchSheetData(sheetId, 'ìƒí™©ë°ì´í„°!A:Z', apiKey);
      situations = convertRowsToObjects(situationRows);
    } catch (error) {
      console.warn('ìƒí™© ë°ì´í„° ì‹œíŠ¸ë¥¼ ì°¾ì„ ìˆ˜ ì—†ìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤. ê¸°ì¡´ ë°ì´í„°ë¥¼ ìœ ì§€í•©ë‹ˆë‹¤.');
      // ê¸°ì¡´ situations.json íŒŒì¼ ìœ ì§€
      if (fs.existsSync('src/data/situations.json')) {
        const existingData = JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync('src/data/situations.json', 'utf8'));
        situations = existingData.situations || [];
      }
    }
    
    // ë°ì´í„° ê²€ì¦
    const errors = validatePolicyData(policies);
    if (errors.length > 0) {
      console.error('âŒ ë°ì´í„° ê²€ì¦ ì‹¤íŒ¨:');
      errors.forEach(error => console.error(`  - ${error}`));
      process.exit(1);
    }
    
    // JSON íŒŒì¼ ìƒì„±
    const policiesData = { policies };
    const situationsData = { situations };
    
    fs.writeFileSync('src/data/policies.json', JSON.stringify(policiesData, null, 2));
    if (situations.length > 0) {
      fs.writeFileSync('src/data/situations.json', JSON.stringify(situationsData, null, 2));
    }
    
    console.log(`âœ… ì„±ê³µì ìœ¼ë¡œ ì—…ë°ì´íŠ¸ë˜ì—ˆìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤:`);
    console.log(`  - ì •ì±… ë°ì´í„°: ${policies.length}ê°œ`);
    console.log(`  - ìƒí™© ë°ì´í„°: ${situations.length}ê°œ`);
    
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('âŒ ì—…ë°ì´íŠ¸ ì‹¤íŒ¨:', error.message);
    process.exit(1);
  }
}

main();

```

## ğŸ”§ **ê·¼ë³¸ì  í•´ê²°: Force Push ì˜µì…˜ ì¶”ê°€**

```github-actions-workflow
name: Update Policies from Google Sheets

on:
  schedule:
    # ë§¤ì¼ ì˜¤ì „ 9ì‹œì— ìë™ ì‹¤í–‰ (KST ê¸°ì¤€)
    - cron: '0 0 * * *'
  workflow_dispatch:
    # ìˆ˜ë™ ì‹¤í–‰ ê°€ëŠ¥

jobs:
  update-data:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    permissions:
      contents: write
    
    steps:
    - name: Checkout repository
      uses: actions/checkout@v4
      with:
        fetch-depth: 0
        token: ${{ secrets.GITHUB_TOKEN }}
      
    - name: Setup Node.js
      uses: actions/setup-node@v4
      with:
        node-version: '18'
        
    - name: Install dependencies
      run: |
        npm install axios csv-parser
        
    - name: Download and convert Google Sheets data
      env:
        SHEETS_API_KEY: ${{ secrets.GOOGLE_SHEETS_API_KEY }}
        SHEETS_ID: ${{ secrets.GOOGLE_SHEETS_ID }}
      run: |
        node scripts/update-policies.js
        
    - name: Commit and push if changes
      uses: stefanzweifel/git-auto-commit-action@v5
      with:
        commit_message: 'ğŸ“Š ì •ì±… ë°ì´í„° ìë™ ì—…ë°ì´íŠ¸'
        file_pattern: 'src/data/*'
        commit_user_name: 'github-actions[bot]'
        commit_user_email: 'github-actions[bot]@users.noreply.github.com'
        push_options: '--force'

```

âš ï¸ **force pushëŠ” ìœ„í—˜í•  ìˆ˜ ìˆìœ¼ë¯€ë¡œ** ë” ì•ˆì „í•œ ëŒ€ì•ˆë„ ì¤€ë¹„í•˜ê² ìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤:

```github-actions-workflow
name: Update Policies from Google Sheets

on:
  schedule:
    # ë§¤ì¼ ì˜¤ì „ 9ì‹œì— ìë™ ì‹¤í–‰ (KST ê¸°ì¤€)
    - cron: '0 0 * * *'
  workflow_dispatch:
    # ìˆ˜ë™ ì‹¤í–‰ ê°€ëŠ¥

jobs:
  update-data:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    permissions:
      contents: write
    
    steps:
    - name: Checkout repository
      uses: actions/checkout@v4
      with:
        fetch-depth: 0
        token: ${{ secrets.GITHUB_TOKEN }}
      
    - name: Setup Node.js
      uses: actions/setup-node@v4
      with:
        node-version: '18'
        
    - name: Install dependencies
      run: |
        npm install axios csv-parser
        
    - name: Download and convert Google Sheets data
      env:
        SHEETS_API_KEY: ${{ secrets.GOOGLE_SHEETS_API_KEY }}
        SHEETS_ID: ${{ secrets.GOOGLE_SHEETS_ID }}
      run: |
        node scripts/update-policies.js
        
    - name: Commit and push if changes
      run: |
        git config --local user.email "github-actions[bot]@users.noreply.github.com"
        git config --local user.name "github-actions[bot]"
        
        # ë³€ê²½ì‚¬í•­ì´ ìˆëŠ”ì§€ í™•ì¸
        git add src/data/
        
        if git diff --staged --quiet; then
          echo "ë³€ê²½ì‚¬í•­ì´ ì—†ìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤."
          exit 0
        fi
        
        # ì»¤ë°‹ ìƒì„±
        git commit -m "ğŸ“Š ì •ì±… ë°ì´í„° ìë™ ì—…ë°ì´íŠ¸ $(date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M')"
        
        # ì•ˆì „í•œ pushë¥¼ ìœ„í•œ ê°•ë ¥í•œ ì¬ì‹œë„ ë¡œì§
        MAX_RETRIES=5
        for i in $(seq 1 $MAX_RETRIES); do
          echo "Push ì‹œë„ $i/$MAX_RETRIES"
          
          # ìµœì‹  ìƒíƒœë¡œ ë¦¬ë² ì´ìŠ¤
          if git fetch origin main && git rebase origin/main; then
            # ë¦¬ë² ì´ìŠ¤ ì„±ê³µì‹œ í‘¸ì‹œ ì‹œë„
            if git push origin main; then
              echo "âœ… Push ì„±ê³µ!"
              exit 0
            fi
          else
            echo "âš ï¸ ë¦¬ë² ì´ìŠ¤ ì‹¤íŒ¨, force push ì‹œë„"
            # ë¦¬ë² ì´ìŠ¤ ì‹¤íŒ¨ì‹œ force push (ë°ì´í„° íŒŒì¼ë§Œ ë³€ê²½í•˜ë¯€ë¡œ ì•ˆì „)
            if git push --force-with-lease origin main; then
              echo "âœ… Force push ì„±ê³µ!"
              exit 0
            fi
          fi
          
          if [ $i -eq $MAX_RETRIES ]; then
            echo "âŒ $MAX_RETRIES ì‹œë„ í›„ ì‹¤íŒ¨"
            exit 1
          fi
          
          echo "â³ 10ì´ˆ ëŒ€ê¸° í›„ ì¬ì‹œë„..."
          sleep 10
        done

```

## âœ… **ê°•ë ¥í•œ Git Push ì†”ë£¨ì…˜ ì ìš© ì™„ë£Œ!**

### **ìƒˆë¡œìš´ ì¬ì‹œë„ ë¡œì§:**

1. **1ì°¨ ì‹œë„**: `fetch â†’ rebase â†’ push` (ì •ìƒì ì¸ ë°©ë²•)
2. **2ì°¨ ì‹œë„**: `--force-with-lease` (ì•ˆì „í•œ force push)
3. **ìµœëŒ€ 5íšŒ ì¬ì‹œë„** + **10ì´ˆ ê°„ê²©**
4. **ìƒì„¸í•œ ë¡œê·¸**ë¡œ ì–´ë–¤ ë‹¨ê³„ì—ì„œ ì„±ê³µ/ì‹¤íŒ¨í–ˆëŠ”ì§€ í™•ì¸

### **`--force-with-lease`ì˜ ì¥ì :**
- **ì•ˆì „**: ë‹¤ë¥¸ ì‚¬ëŒì´ í‘¸ì‹œí•œ ë‚´ìš©ì„ ë®ì–´ì“°ì§€ ì•ŠìŒ
- **íš¨ê³¼ì **: Git íˆìŠ¤í† ë¦¬ ë¶ˆì¼ì¹˜ í•´ê²°
- **ì í•©**: ë°ì´í„° íŒŒì¼ë§Œ ë³€ê²½í•˜ëŠ” ìë™í™”ì— ìµœì 

---

## ğŸš€ **ì´ì œ ìµœì¢… í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸**

**GitHub Actionsì—ì„œ ì›Œí¬í”Œë¡œìš°ë¥¼ ì¬ì‹¤í–‰í•´ë³´ì„¸ìš”!**

í›Œë¥­í•©ë‹ˆë‹¤! ğŸ‰ ìë™í™”ê°€ ì„±ê³µí–ˆê³  ë””ë²„ê¹… í˜ì´ì§€ë„ ì •ìƒ ì‘ë™í•˜ë„¤ìš”!

## ğŸ” **ë§¤ì¹­ ê²°ê³¼ ë¶„ì„**

ë””ë²„ê¹… ê²°ê³¼ë¥¼ ë³´ë‹ˆ **ë§¤ì¹­ ì ìˆ˜ê°€ ëª¨ë‘ 0ì **ìœ¼ë¡œ ë‚˜ì˜¤ëŠ” ë¬¸ì œê°€ ì—¬ì „íˆ ìˆìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤. 

### **í˜„ì¬ ìƒí™©:**
- âœ… **ìë™í™” ì„±ê³µ**: Google Sheets â†’ JSON ë³€í™˜ ì™„ë£Œ
- âœ… **ë°ì´í„° íŒŒì‹±**: íƒœê·¸ë“¤ì´ ì˜¬ë°”ë¥´ê²Œ í‘œì‹œë¨
- âŒ **ë§¤ì¹­ ë¡œì§**: ì—¬ì „íˆ 0ì  (íƒœê·¸ ë§¤ì¹­ì´ ì•ˆë¨)

### **ë°œê²¬ëœ ë¬¸ì œì :**

#### **1. íƒœê·¸ ë¶ˆì¼ì¹˜ ë¬¸ì œ**
- **ì„ íƒëœ ìƒí™©ì˜ íƒœê·¸**: `["ìì·¨", "ë…ë¦½", "ìƒí™œë¹„", "ì£¼ê±°ë¹„", "ê°€êµ¬", "ìƒí™œìš©í’ˆ"]`
- **ì •ì±… íƒœê·¸**: `["ì£¼ê±°", "ì²­ë…„", "ì›”ì„¸", "ìƒí™œë¹„", "ë…ë¦½", "ë³´ì¦ê¸ˆ"]`
- **ë§¤ì¹­ë˜ëŠ” íƒœê·¸**: `"ìƒí™œë¹„"`, `"ë…ë¦½"` (2ê°œ)
- **ì˜ˆìƒ ì ìˆ˜**: 2 Ã— 10 = 20ì  (í•˜ì§€ë§Œ ì‹¤ì œë¡œëŠ” 0ì )

#### **2. ë§¤ì¹­ ë¡œì§ ì˜¤ë¥˜ ê°€ëŠ¥ì„±**
í•˜ë“œì½”ë”©ëœ ìƒí™© íƒœê·¸ì™€ ì‹¤ì œ ë°ì´í„°ì˜ íƒœê·¸ê°€ ì¼ì¹˜í•˜ì§€ ì•Šì„ ìˆ˜ ìˆìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤.

## ğŸ”§ **í•´ê²° ë°©ì•ˆ**

### **ë°©ì•ˆ 1: ì‹¤ì œ ë§¤ì¹­ ê³¼ì • ë””ë²„ê¹…**

```typescript
import { Policy, SituationId, SortOption, CategoryId } from '@/types';

/**
 * ì •ì±…ê³¼ ì„ íƒëœ ìƒí™© ê°„ì˜ ë§¤ì¹­ ì ìˆ˜ë¥¼ ê³„ì‚°í•©ë‹ˆë‹¤.
 * 
 * ë§¤ì¹­ ìš°ì„ ìˆœìœ„:
 * 1. íƒœê·¸ ë§¤ì¹­ ê°œìˆ˜ (ê°€ì¥ ì¤‘ìš”)
 * 2. ìƒí™© ë§¤ì¹­ ê°œìˆ˜
 * 3. ë§ˆê° ì„ë°• ë³´ë„ˆìŠ¤ (+1ì , 30ì¼ ì´ë‚´)
 */
export function calculateMatchScore(
  selectedSituations: SituationId[],
  policy: Policy
): number {
  let score = 0;

  // 1. íƒœê·¸ ë§¤ì¹­ ì ìˆ˜ ê³„ì‚°
  const selectedTags = new Set<string>();
  selectedSituations.forEach(situationId => {
    // SITUATIONSì—ì„œ í•´ë‹¹ ìƒí™©ì˜ íƒœê·¸ë“¤ì„ ê°€ì ¸ì™€ì„œ ì¶”ê°€
    const situationTags = getSituationTags(situationId);
    situationTags.forEach(tag => selectedTags.add(tag));
  });

  // ë””ë²„ê¹…: íƒœê·¸ ë§¤ì¹­ ê³¼ì • ë¡œê·¸
  console.log('ğŸ” ë§¤ì¹­ ë””ë²„ê¹…:', {
    selectedSituations,
    selectedTags: Array.from(selectedTags),
    policyId: policy.id,
    policyTags: policy.tags,
    policySituations: policy.situations,
    tagType: typeof policy.tags,
    situationType: typeof policy.situations,
    isTagsArray: Array.isArray(policy.tags),
    isSituationsArray: Array.isArray(policy.situations)
  });

  // ì„ íƒëœ íƒœê·¸ì™€ ì •ì±… íƒœê·¸ ê°„ì˜ ë§¤ì¹­ ê°œìˆ˜ ê³„ì‚°
  const tagMatches = policy.tags.filter(tag => selectedTags.has(tag)).length;
  score += tagMatches * 10; // íƒœê·¸ ë§¤ì¹­ì€ ë†’ì€ ê°€ì¤‘ì¹˜

  // 2. ìƒí™© ë§¤ì¹­ ì ìˆ˜ ê³„ì‚°
  const situationMatches = policy.situations.filter(situation => 
    selectedSituations.includes(situation)
  ).length;
  score += situationMatches * 5; // ìƒí™© ë§¤ì¹­ì€ ì¤‘ê°„ ê°€ì¤‘ì¹˜

  // 3. ë§ˆê° ì„ë°• ë³´ë„ˆìŠ¤ (30ì¼ ì´ë‚´)
  const today = new Date();
  const deadline = new Date(policy.deadline);
  const daysUntilDeadline = Math.ceil((deadline.getTime() - today.getTime()) / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24));
  
  if (daysUntilDeadline <= 30 && daysUntilDeadline > 0) {
    score += 1; // ë§ˆê° ì„ë°• ë³´ë„ˆìŠ¤
  }

  console.log('ğŸ” ì ìˆ˜ ê³„ì‚°:', {
    policyId: policy.id,
    tagMatches,
    situationMatches,
    deadlineBonus: (daysUntilDeadline <= 30 && daysUntilDeadline > 0) ? 1 : 0,
    totalScore: score
  });

  return score;
}

/**
 * ìƒí™© IDì— í•´ë‹¹í•˜ëŠ” íƒœê·¸ë“¤ì„ ë°˜í™˜í•©ë‹ˆë‹¤.
 */
function getSituationTags(situationId: SituationId): string[] {
  const situationTags: Record<SituationId, string[]> = {
    independence: ['ìì·¨', 'ë…ë¦½', 'ìƒí™œë¹„', 'ì£¼ê±°ë¹„', 'ê°€êµ¬', 'ìƒí™œìš©í’ˆ'],
    'job-seeking': ['êµ¬ì§', 'ì·¨ì—…', 'ì´ë ¥ì„œ', 'ë©´ì ‘', 'êµìœ¡', 'í›ˆë ¨'],
    'after-resignation': ['í‡´ì‚¬', 'ì „ì§', 'ì°½ì—…', 'êµìœ¡', 'ìê²©ì¦', 'ì¬ì·¨ì—…'],
    'childcare-prep': ['ìœ¡ì•„', 'ì„ì‹ ', 'ì¶œì‚°', 'ë³´ìœ¡', 'êµìœ¡', 'ë³µì§€'],
    'tax-settlement': ['ì—°ë§ì •ì‚°', 'ì„¸ê¸ˆ', 'í™˜ê¸‰', 'ê³µì œ', 'ì‹ ê³ ', 'ì ˆì„¸'],
    'marriage-prep': ['ê²°í˜¼', 'ì‹ í˜¼', 'í˜¼ë¡€', 'ì‹ í˜¼ë¶€ë¶€', 'ì£¼íƒ', 'ëŒ€ì¶œ']
  };
  
  return situationTags[situationId] || [];
}

/**
 * ì •ì±…ë“¤ì„ í•„í„°ë§í•˜ê³  ì •ë ¬í•©ë‹ˆë‹¤.
 */
export function filterAndSortPolicies(
  policies: Policy[],
  selectedSituations: SituationId[],
  sortOption: SortOption = 'recommended',
  category?: CategoryId
): Policy[] {
  let filteredPolicies = policies;

  // ì¹´í…Œê³ ë¦¬ í•„í„°ë§
  if (category) {
    filteredPolicies = filteredPolicies.filter(policy => policy.category === category);
  }

  // ë§¤ì¹­ ì ìˆ˜ ê³„ì‚°
  const policiesWithScore = filteredPolicies.map(policy => ({
    ...policy,
    matchScore: calculateMatchScore(selectedSituations, policy)
  }));

  // ì •ë ¬ ì ìš©
  switch (sortOption) {
    case 'recommended':
      return policiesWithScore
        .sort((a, b) => b.matchScore - a.matchScore)
        .map(({ matchScore, ...policy }) => policy);

    case 'deadline':
      return policiesWithScore
        .sort((a, b) => {
          const aDeadline = new Date(a.deadline);
          const bDeadline = new Date(b.deadline);
          return aDeadline.getTime() - bDeadline.getTime();
        })
        .map(({ matchScore, ...policy }) => policy);

    case 'latest':
      return policiesWithScore
        .sort((a, b) => {
          const aCreated = new Date(a.createdAt);
          const bCreated = new Date(b.createdAt);
          return bCreated.getTime() - aCreated.getTime();
        })
        .map(({ matchScore, ...policy }) => policy);

    default:
      return policiesWithScore
        .sort((a, b) => b.matchScore - a.matchScore)
        .map(({ matchScore, ...policy }) => policy);
  }
}

/**
 * ì •ì±…ì˜ ë§ˆê°ì¼ê¹Œì§€ ë‚¨ì€ ì¼ìˆ˜ë¥¼ ê³„ì‚°í•©ë‹ˆë‹¤.
 */
export function getDaysUntilDeadline(deadline: string): number {
  const today = new Date();
  const deadlineDate = new Date(deadline);
  const diffTime = deadlineDate.getTime() - today.getTime();
  return Math.ceil(diffTime / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24));
}

/**
 * ë§ˆê° ì„ë°• ì—¬ë¶€ë¥¼ í™•ì¸í•©ë‹ˆë‹¤ (30ì¼ ì´ë‚´).
 */
export function isDeadlineSoon(deadline: string): boolean {
  const daysUntilDeadline = getDaysUntilDeadline(deadline);
  return daysUntilDeadline <= 30 && daysUntilDeadline > 0;
}

/**
 * ë§ˆê° ìƒíƒœë¥¼ ë°˜í™˜í•©ë‹ˆë‹¤.
 */
export function getDeadlineStatus(deadline: string): 'active' | 'soon' | 'expired' {
  const daysUntilDeadline = getDaysUntilDeadline(deadline);
  
  if (daysUntilDeadline < 0) return 'expired';
  if (daysUntilDeadline <= 30) return 'soon';
  return 'active';
} 
```

## ğŸ” **íƒœê·¸ ë¶ˆì¼ì¹˜ ë¬¸ì œ ë°œê²¬!**

### **í•˜ë“œì½”ë”©ëœ ìƒí™© íƒœê·¸ vs ì‹¤ì œ ì •ì±… íƒœê·¸**

#### **ìì·¨ ì‹œì‘ (independence):**
- **í•˜ë“œì½”ë”©ëœ íƒœê·¸**: `["ìì·¨", "ë…ë¦½", "ìƒí™œë¹„", "ì£¼ê±°ë¹„", "ê°€êµ¬", "ìƒí™œìš©í’ˆ"]`
- **ì‹¤ì œ ì •ì±… íƒœê·¸**: `["ì£¼ê±°", "ì²­ë…„", "ì›”ì„¸", "ìƒí™œë¹„", "ë…ë¦½", "ë³´ì¦ê¸ˆ"]`
- **ë§¤ì¹­**: `"ìƒí™œë¹„"`, `"ë…ë¦½"` (2ê°œë§Œ ë§¤ì¹­)

- **í•˜ë“œì½”ë”©ëœ íƒœê·¸**: `["êµ¬ì§", "ì·¨ì—…", "ì´ë ¥ì„œ", "ë©´ì ‘", "êµìœ¡", "í›ˆë ¨"]`
- **ì‹¤ì œ ì •ì±… íƒœê·¸**: `["ì·¨ì—…", "ì²­ë…„", "êµ¬ì§í™œë™", "êµìœ¡", "ìê²©ì¦", "ì¸í„´"]`
- **ë§¤ì¹­**: `"ì·¨ì—…"`, `"êµìœ¡"` (2ê°œë§Œ ë§¤ì¹­)

## ğŸ”§ **í•´ê²° ë°©ì•ˆ 2ê°€ì§€**

### **ë°©ì•ˆ 1: í•˜ë“œì½”ë”©ëœ íƒœê·¸ë¥¼ ì‹¤ì œ ë°ì´í„°ì— ë§ê²Œ ìˆ˜ì •**

```typescript

 * ì •ì±…ê³¼ ì„ íƒëœ ìƒí™© ê°„ì˜ ë§¤ì¹­ ì ìˆ˜ë¥¼ ê³„ì‚°í•©ë‹ˆë‹¤.
 * 
 * ë§¤ì¹­ ìš°ì„ ìˆœìœ„:
 * 1. íƒœê·¸ ë§¤ì¹­ ê°œìˆ˜ (ê°€ì¥ ì¤‘ìš”)
 * 2. ìƒí™© ë§¤ì¹­ ê°œìˆ˜
 * 3. ë§ˆê° ì„ë°• ë³´ë„ˆìŠ¤ (+1ì , 30ì¼ ì´ë‚´)
 */
export function calculateMatchScore(
  selectedSituations: SituationId[],
  policy: Policy
): number {
  let score = 0;

  // 1. íƒœê·¸ ë§¤ì¹­ ì ìˆ˜ ê³„ì‚°
  const selectedTags = new Set<string>();
  selectedSituations.forEach(situationId => {
    // SITUATIONSì—ì„œ í•´ë‹¹ ìƒí™©ì˜ íƒœê·¸ë“¤ì„ ê°€ì ¸ì™€ì„œ ì¶”ê°€
    const situationTags = getSituationTags(situationId);
    situationTags.forEach(tag => selectedTags.add(tag));
  });

  // ë””ë²„ê¹…: íƒœê·¸ ë§¤ì¹­ ê³¼ì • ë¡œê·¸
  console.log('ğŸ” ë§¤ì¹­ ë””ë²„ê¹…:', {
    selectedSituations,
    selectedTags: Array.from(selectedTags),
    policyId: policy.id,
    policyTags: policy.tags,
    policySituations: policy.situations,
    tagType: typeof policy.tags,
    situationType: typeof policy.situations,
    isTagsArray: Array.isArray(policy.tags),
    isSituationsArray: Array.isArray(policy.situations)
  });

  // ì„ íƒëœ íƒœê·¸ì™€ ì •ì±… íƒœê·¸ ê°„ì˜ ë§¤ì¹­ ê°œìˆ˜ ê³„ì‚°
  const tagMatches = policy.tags.filter(tag => selectedTags.has(tag)).length;
  score += tagMatches * 10; // íƒœê·¸ ë§¤ì¹­ì€ ë†’ì€ ê°€ì¤‘ì¹˜

  // 2. ìƒí™© ë§¤ì¹­ ì ìˆ˜ ê³„ì‚°
  const situationMatches = policy.situations.filter(situation => 
    selectedSituations.includes(situation)
  ).length;
  score += situationMatches * 5; // ìƒí™© ë§¤ì¹­ì€ ì¤‘ê°„ ê°€ì¤‘ì¹˜

  // 3. ë§ˆê° ì„ë°• ë³´ë„ˆìŠ¤ (30ì¼ ì´ë‚´)
  const today = new Date();
  const deadline = new Date(policy.deadline);
  const daysUntilDeadline = Math.ceil((deadline.getTime() - today.getTime()) / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24));
  
  if (daysUntilDeadline <= 30 && daysUntilDeadline > 0) {
    score += 1; // ë§ˆê° ì„ë°• ë³´ë„ˆìŠ¤
  }

  console.log('ğŸ” ì ìˆ˜ ê³„ì‚°:', {
    policyId: policy.id,
    tagMatches,
    situationMatches,
    deadlineBonus: (daysUntilDeadline <= 30 && daysUntilDeadline > 0) ? 1 : 0,
    totalScore: score
  });

  return score;
}

/**
 * ìƒí™© IDì— í•´ë‹¹í•˜ëŠ” íƒœê·¸ë“¤ì„ ë°˜í™˜í•©ë‹ˆë‹¤.
 */
function getSituationTags(situationId: SituationId): string[] {
  // ì‹¤ì œ ì •ì±… ë°ì´í„°ì—ì„œ ìì£¼ ì‚¬ìš©ë˜ëŠ” íƒœê·¸ë“¤ë¡œ ì—…ë°ì´íŠ¸
  const situationTags: Record<SituationId, string[]> = {
    independence: ['ì£¼ê±°', 'ì²­ë…„', 'ì›”ì„¸', 'ìƒí™œë¹„', 'ë…ë¦½', 'ë³´ì¦ê¸ˆ', 'ìì·¨', 'ì£¼ê±°ë¹„'],
    'job-seeking': ['ì·¨ì—…', 'ì²­ë…„', 'êµ¬ì§í™œë™', 'êµìœ¡', 'ìê²©ì¦', 'ì¸í„´', 'êµ¬ì§', 'í›ˆë ¨'],
    'after-resignation': ['ì‹¤ì—…ê¸‰ì—¬', 'ì´ì§', 'ì¬ì·¨ì—…', 'êµìœ¡', 'ì§ì—…í›ˆë ¨', 'ìƒí™œë¹„', 'í‡´ì‚¬', 'ì „ì§'],
    'childcare-prep': ['ìœ¡ì•„', 'ëŒë´„', 'ì¶œì‚°', 'ë³´ìœ¡', 'ì–´ë¦°ì´ì§‘', 'ì˜ë£Œ', 'ì„ì‹ ', 'ë³µì§€'],
    'tax-settlement': ['ì„¸ê¸ˆ', 'ê³µì œ', 'í™˜ê¸‰', 'ì†Œë“', 'ì ˆì„¸', 'ê·¼ë¡œì†Œë“', 'ì—°ë§ì •ì‚°'],
    'marriage-prep': ['ê²°í˜¼', 'ì‹ í˜¼', 'í˜¼ë¡€', 'ì‹ í˜¼ë¶€ë¶€', 'ì£¼íƒ', 'ëŒ€ì¶œ', 'ëŒ€ì¶œê¸ˆ']
  };
  
  return situationTags[situationId] || [];
}

/**
 * ì •ì±…ë“¤ì„ í•„í„°ë§í•˜ê³  ì •ë ¬í•©ë‹ˆë‹¤.
 */
export function filterAndSortPolicies(
  policies: Policy[],
  selectedSituations: SituationId[],
  sortOption: SortOption = 'recommended',
  category?: CategoryId
): Policy[] {
  let filteredPolicies = policies;

  // ì¹´í…Œê³ ë¦¬ í•„í„°ë§
  if (category) {
    filteredPolicies = filteredPolicies.filter(policy => policy.category === category);
  }

  // ë§¤ì¹­ ì ìˆ˜ ê³„ì‚°
  const policiesWithScore = filteredPolicies.map(policy => ({
    ...policy,
    matchScore: calculateMatchScore(selectedSituations, policy)
  }));

  // ì •ë ¬ ì ìš©
  switch (sortOption) {
    case 'recommended':
      return policiesWithScore
        .sort((a, b) => b.matchScore - a.matchScore)
        .map(({ matchScore, ...policy }) => policy);

    case 'deadline':
      return policiesWithScore
        .sort((a, b) => {
          const aDeadline = new Date(a.deadline);
          const bDeadline = new Date(b.deadline);
          return aDeadline.getTime() - bDeadline.getTime();
        })
        .map(({ matchScore, ...policy }) => policy);

    case 'latest':
      return policiesWithScore
        .sort((a, b) => {
          const aCreated = new Date(a.createdAt);
          const bCreated = new Date(b.createdAt);
          return bCreated.getTime() - aCreated.getTime();
        })
        .map(({ matchScore, ...policy }) => policy);

    default:
      return policiesWithScore
        .sort((a, b) => b.matchScore - a.matchScore)
        .map(({ matchScore, ...policy }) => policy);
  }
}

/**
 * ì •ì±…ì˜ ë§ˆê°ì¼ê¹Œì§€ ë‚¨ì€ ì¼ìˆ˜ë¥¼ ê³„ì‚°í•©ë‹ˆë‹¤.
 */
export function getDaysUntilDeadline(deadline: string): number {
  const today = new Date();
  const deadlineDate = new Date(deadline);
  const diffTime = deadlineDate.getTime() - today.getTime();
  return Math.ceil(diffTime / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24));
}

/**
 * ë§ˆê° ì„ë°• ì—¬ë¶€ë¥¼ í™•ì¸í•©ë‹ˆë‹¤ (30ì¼ ì´ë‚´).
 */
export function isDeadlineSoon(deadline: string): boolean {
  const daysUntilDeadline = getDaysUntilDeadline(deadline);
  return daysUntilDeadline <= 30 && daysUntilDeadline > 0;
}

 * ë§ˆê° ìƒíƒœë¥¼ ë°˜í™˜í•©ë‹ˆë‹¤.

  const daysUntilDeadline = getDaysUntilDeadline(deadline);
  
  if (daysUntilDeadline < 0) return 'expired';
  if (daysUntilDeadline <= 30) return 'soon';
  return 'active';
}
```

ì´ì œ ë””ë²„ê¹… í˜ì´ì§€ë„ ì—…ë°ì´íŠ¸í•˜ê² ìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤:

```typescriptreact
'use client';

import { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import { Policy, SituationId } from '@/types';
import { loadPolicies } from '@/lib/utils';
import { calculateMatchScore } from '@/lib/matching';

// ì‹¤ì œ ì •ì±… ë°ì´í„°ì— ë§ì¶˜ ìƒí™© íƒœê·¸ (ë§¤ì¹­ ë¡œì§ê³¼ ë™ì¼)
const SITUATION_TAGS: Record<SituationId, string[]> = {
  independence: ['ì£¼ê±°', 'ì²­ë…„', 'ì›”ì„¸', 'ìƒí™œë¹„', 'ë…ë¦½', 'ë³´ì¦ê¸ˆ', 'ìì·¨', 'ì£¼ê±°ë¹„'],
  'job-seeking': ['ì·¨ì—…', 'ì²­ë…„', 'êµ¬ì§í™œë™', 'êµìœ¡', 'ìê²©ì¦', 'ì¸í„´', 'êµ¬ì§', 'í›ˆë ¨'],
  'after-resignation': ['ì‹¤ì—…ê¸‰ì—¬', 'ì´ì§', 'ì¬ì·¨ì—…', 'êµìœ¡', 'ì§ì—…í›ˆë ¨', 'ìƒí™œë¹„', 'í‡´ì‚¬', 'ì „ì§'],
  'childcare-prep': ['ìœ¡ì•„', 'ëŒë´„', 'ì¶œì‚°', 'ë³´ìœ¡', 'ì–´ë¦°ì´ì§‘', 'ì˜ë£Œ', 'ì„ì‹ ', 'ë³µì§€'],
  'tax-settlement': ['ì„¸ê¸ˆ', 'ê³µì œ', 'í™˜ê¸‰', 'ì†Œë“', 'ì ˆì„¸', 'ê·¼ë¡œì†Œë“', 'ì—°ë§ì •ì‚°'],
  'marriage-prep': ['ê²°í˜¼', 'ì‹ í˜¼', 'í˜¼ë¡€', 'ì‹ í˜¼ë¶€ë¶€', 'ì£¼íƒ', 'ëŒ€ì¶œ', 'ëŒ€ì¶œê¸ˆ']
};

const SITUATION_LABELS = {
  independence: 'ìì·¨ ì‹œì‘',
  'job-seeking': 'êµ¬ì§ ì¤‘',
  'after-resignation': 'í‡´ì‚¬ í›„',
  'childcare-prep': 'ìœ¡ì•„ ì¤€ë¹„',
  'tax-settlement': 'ì—°ë§ì •ì‚°',
  'marriage-prep': 'ê²°í˜¼ ì¤€ë¹„'
};

export default function DebugPage() {
  const [policies, setPolicies] = useState<Policy[]>([]);
  const [selectedSituations, setSelectedSituations] = useState<SituationId[]>(['independence']);
  const [debugResults, setDebugResults] = useState<any[]>([]);

  useEffect(() => {
    const allPolicies = loadPolicies();
    setPolicies(allPolicies);
  }, []);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (policies.length > 0) {
      runDebugTest();
    }
  }, [policies, selectedSituations]);

  const runDebugTest = () => {
    // ì„ íƒëœ ìƒí™©ë“¤ì˜ íƒœê·¸ í•©ì¹˜ê¸°
    const selectedTags = new Set<string>();
    selectedSituations.forEach(situationId => {
      SITUATION_TAGS[situationId].forEach(tag => selectedTags.add(tag));
    });

    const results = policies.map(policy => {
      const score = calculateMatchScore(selectedSituations, policy);
      
      // íƒœê·¸ ë§¤ì¹­ ë¶„ì„
      const tagMatches = policy.tags.filter(tag => selectedTags.has(tag));
      const tagScore = tagMatches.length * 10;

      // ìƒí™© ë§¤ì¹­ ë¶„ì„  
      const situationMatches = policy.situations.filter(situation => 
        selectedSituations.includes(situation)
      );
      const situationScore = situationMatches.length * 5;

      // ë§ˆê° ì„ë°• ë³´ë„ˆìŠ¤
      const today = new Date();
      const deadline = new Date(policy.deadline);
      const daysUntilDeadline = Math.ceil((deadline.getTime() - today.getTime()) / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24));
      const deadlineBonus = (daysUntilDeadline <= 30 && daysUntilDeadline > 0) ? 1 : 0;

      return {
        policy,
        totalScore: score,
        breakdown: {
          tagMatches,
          tagScore,
          situationMatches,
          situationScore,
          deadlineBonus,
          daysUntilDeadline
        }
      };
    }).sort((a, b) => b.totalScore - a.totalScore);

    setDebugResults(results);
  };

  const toggleSituation = (situationId: SituationId) => {
    setSelectedSituations(prev => {
      if (prev.includes(situationId)) {
        return prev.filter(id => id !== situationId);
      } else {
        return [...prev, situationId];
      }
    });
  };

  const selectedTagsArray = Array.from(
    new Set(selectedSituations.flatMap(id => SITUATION_TAGS[id]))
  );

  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen bg-gray-50 p-8">
      <div className="max-w-6xl mx-auto">
        <h1 className="text-3xl font-bold text-gray-900 mb-8">ğŸ” ë§¤ì¹­ ì•Œê³ ë¦¬ì¦˜ ë””ë²„ê¹…</h1>
        
        {/* ìƒí™© ì„ íƒê¸° */}
        <div className="bg-white rounded-lg p-6 mb-8 shadow">
          <h2 className="text-xl font-semibold mb-4">í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸í•  ìƒí™© ì„ íƒ</h2>
          <div className="grid grid-cols-2 md:grid-cols-3 gap-4">
            {Object.entries(SITUATION_LABELS).map(([id, label]) => (
              <button
                key={id}
                onClick={() => toggleSituation(id as SituationId)}
                className={`p-3 rounded-lg border-2 text-left transition-colors ${
                  selectedSituations.includes(id as SituationId)
                    ? 'border-blue-500 bg-blue-50 text-blue-700'
                    : 'border-gray-200 hover:border-gray-300'
                }`}
              >
                <div className="font-medium">{label}</div>
                <div className="text-sm text-gray-500">{id}</div>
              </button>
            ))}
          </div>

          {/* ì„ íƒëœ íƒœê·¸ í‘œì‹œ */}
          <div className="mt-4">
            <h3 className="font-medium text-gray-700 mb-2">ì„ íƒëœ ìƒí™©ì˜ íƒœê·¸ë“¤:</h3>
            <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-2">
              {selectedTagsArray.map(tag => (
                <span key={tag} className="px-2 py-1 bg-blue-100 text-blue-700 rounded text-sm">
                  {tag}
                </span>
              ))}
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>

        {/* ë””ë²„ê¹… ê²°ê³¼ */}
        <div className="space-y-4">
          <h2 className="text-xl font-semibold">ë§¤ì¹­ ê²°ê³¼ (ì´ {debugResults.length}ê°œ ì •ì±…)</h2>
          
          {debugResults.map(({ policy, totalScore, breakdown }, index) => (
            <div key={policy.id} className="bg-white rounded-lg p-6 shadow">
              <div className="flex justify-between items-start mb-4">
                <div>
                  <h3 className="text-lg font-semibold text-gray-900">{policy.title}</h3>
                  <p className="text-sm text-gray-600">{policy.id} | {policy.category}</p>
                </div>
                <div className="text-right">
                  <div className="text-2xl font-bold text-blue-600">{totalScore}ì </div>
                  <div className="text-sm text-gray-500">#{index + 1}</div>
                </div>
              </div>

              {/* ì ìˆ˜ ë¶„ì„ */}
              <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-3 gap-4 mb-4">
                <div className="bg-green-50 p-3 rounded">
                  <div className="font-medium text-green-800">íƒœê·¸ ë§¤ì¹­</div>
                  <div className="text-green-600">{breakdown.tagScore}ì  ({breakdown.tagMatches.length}ê°œ ë§¤ì¹­)</div>
                  <div className="text-xs text-green-600 mt-1">
                    {breakdown.tagMatches.join(', ') || 'ë§¤ì¹­ ì—†ìŒ'}
                  </div>
                </div>

                <div className="bg-blue-50 p-3 rounded">
                  <div className="font-medium text-blue-800">ìƒí™© ë§¤ì¹­</div>
                  <div className="text-blue-600">{breakdown.situationScore}ì  ({breakdown.situationMatches.length}ê°œ ë§¤ì¹­)</div>
                  <div className="text-xs text-blue-600 mt-1">
                    {breakdown.situationMatches.join(', ') || 'ë§¤ì¹­ ì—†ìŒ'}
                  </div>
                </div>

                <div className="bg-orange-50 p-3 rounded">
                  <div className="font-medium text-orange-800">ë§ˆê° ë³´ë„ˆìŠ¤</div>
                  <div className="text-orange-600">{breakdown.deadlineBonus}ì </div>
                  <div className="text-xs text-orange-600 mt-1">
                    {breakdown.daysUntilDeadline}ì¼ ë‚¨ìŒ
                  </div>
                </div>
              </div>

              {/* ì •ì±… íƒœê·¸ */}
              <div>
                <div className="font-medium text-gray-700 mb-2">ì •ì±… íƒœê·¸:</div>
                <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-2">
                  {policy.tags.map(tag => {
                    const isMatched = selectedTagsArray.includes(tag);
                    return (
                      <span 
                        key={tag} 
                        className={`px-2 py-1 rounded text-sm ${
                          isMatched 
                            ? 'bg-green-100 text-green-700 font-medium' 
                            : 'bg-gray-100 text-gray-600'
                        }`}
                      >
                        {tag}
                      </span>
                    );
                  })}
                </div>
              </div>
            </div>
          ))}
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

```

```typescript
  score += 1; // ë§ˆê° ì„ë°• ë³´ë„ˆìŠ¤
```

## ğŸ’¡ **í•´ê²° ë°©ì•ˆ 2ê°€ì§€:**

### **ë°©ì•ˆ 1: ë§ˆê° ê¸°ì¤€ ì™„í™” (ì¶”ì²œ)**

```typescript
  score += 1;
```

```typescript
  score += 3; // ì„ë°•

  score += 1; // ì—¬ìœ
```

**ì–´ë–¤ ë°©í–¥ìœ¼ë¡œ ìˆ˜ì •í•˜ì‹œê² ìŠµë‹ˆê¹Œ?** 

1. ë§ˆê° ê¸°ì¤€ì„ 30ì¼ â†’ 90ì¼ë¡œ ëŠ˜ë¦¬ê¸°

```typescript

  score += 3; // ì„ë°•
} else if (daysUntilDeadline <= 90 && daysUntilDeadline > 0) {
  score += 1; // ì—¬ìœ 
}
```

**User**

**Cursor**

ë„¤! ë§ˆê° ê¸°ì¤€ì„ 90ì¼ë¡œ ëŠ˜ë¦¬ê³  ë‹¨ê³„ë³„ ë³´ë„ˆìŠ¤ ì‹œìŠ¤í…œì„ ë„ì…í•˜ê² ìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤.

```typescript
  // ë§ˆê°ì¼ ë‹¨ê³„ë³„ ë³´ë„ˆìŠ¤ (90ì¼ ì´ë‚´)
  const today = new Date();
  const deadline = new Date(policy.deadline);
  const daysUntilDeadline = Math.ceil((deadline.getTime() - today.getTime()) / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24));
  
  let deadlineBonus = 0;
  if (daysUntilDeadline <= 7 && daysUntilDeadline > 0) {
    deadlineBonus = 5; // ê¸´ê¸‰ (1ì£¼ì¼ ì´ë‚´)
    score += deadlineBonus;

    deadlineBonus = 3; // ì„ë°• (1ê°œì›” ì´ë‚´)
    score += deadlineBonus;

    deadlineBonus = 1; // ì—¬ìœ  (3ê°œì›” ì´ë‚´)
    score += deadlineBonus;

  console.log('ğŸ” ì ìˆ˜ ê³„ì‚°:', {
    policyId: policy.id,
    tagMatches,
    situationMatches,
    daysUntilDeadline,
    deadlineBonus,
```
